Saito Explains the Content of the Five-Minister Conference 32

(Tokyo) Today, Prime Minister Saito met with a group of reporters at his official residence and made the following statement: It is difficult to predict when the Five-Minister Conference will conclude. I hope it will be after the end of the grand military exercises. However, this conference is not necessarily a conference that must achieve a certain outcome; it is merely a forum for each participant to express their opinions. Initially, it was intended for each relevant minister to hear about policies regarding national defense, finance, and diplomacy. Therefore, it has no direct relationship with the budget. However, the outcome may involve the budget. Society seems to be paying close attention to this conference, but it is not of great importance. The scope of discussion now covers national defense, finance, and diplomacy. If it involves other ministries, relevant ministers will also be invited to attend. Rumors that the military, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs hold conflicting opinions are untrue. The decisions made at the Five-Minister Conference may be used as material for national policy, but they will not directly become national policy. What is more difficult than the Five-Minister Conference is the upcoming Cabinet deliberation on the budget. Regarding the verdicts in the May 15th Incident, although young naval officers may have various opinions, once the military court has made a decision, what else is there to say? Regarding Admiral Osumi, there are indeed rumors, but I hope he will dedicate himself to the country. (Fourteenth dispatch from the Electric Communication)

(Tokyo) After yesterday's regular cabinet meeting, Prime Minister Saito specifically retained Home Minister Yamamoto and Finance Minister Takahashi for a long meeting. Judging from this meeting, Prime Minister Saito initially attempted to establish a unified national policy, targeting 1935, encompassing diplomacy, national defense, and finance. However, the conference resulted in conflicting opinions regarding national defense and diplomacy, particularly concerning the issue of concluding a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union, which led to a stalemate. Therefore, at the next Five-Minister Conference on the 16th, opinions will continue to be exchanged on this point, believing that (1) under the current international situation, it is not the time to determine fixed and concrete diplomatic policies, (2) regarding national defense issues, there is no objection to the Navy's Second Replenishment Plan. At the same time, regarding the Army's expenses, if the Army authorities' proposed national defense plan has a predictable basis, their demands must also be accommodated to ensure that national defense capabilities are without regret. Yesterday, this intent was reported to Home Minister Yamamoto, seeking his understanding. Prime Minister Saito's future direction for the Five-Minister Conference is that if a conclusion cannot be reached at the 16th meeting, which focuses on relations with Russia, he plans to convene two or three more meetings and then suspend it, and then reopen it as necessary. It is reported that the relevant ministers have all agreed on this. On the other hand, Minister of Railways Mitsuchi told Finance Minister Takahashi that the recent Five-Minister Conference, especially the movements of the military related to it, have caused widespread anxiety in the world. He asked what the content of the conference was. Finance Minister Takahashi replied that even if the Five-Minister Conference fails to reach a conclusion, there will be no other anxieties in the political situation. (Fourteenth dispatch from the Electric Communication)

Page 9

President Roosevelt States: America Values Peace Above All; Resolutely Opposes War; Does Not Embrace Territorial Expansionism; Has Absolutely No Ambition to Covet Neighboring Countries 33

(Washington) President Roosevelt delivered a radio address, stating that if the imperialist nations threatening world peace wish to eliminate their violence and unite with countries dedicated to peace, they must be spiritually influenced and integrated. Roosevelt also said, "Actions that endanger peace will never originate from the United States. The entire American people oppose war. The American nation has no intention of invading neighboring countries to expand its own territory. Mexico, Canada, and Cuba are all neighbors of the United States. Not only do we have no intention of annexing them, but the United States does not even consider laying a finger on an inch of their soil." In conclusion, he also said, "Most countries in the world must also think this way. The world crisis should be resolved, but it cannot be achieved in a single day or year." (Thirteenth dispatch from Havas)

American Public Opinion Advocates US-Australia Alliance to Restrain Japan; Promotes Solidarity of English-Speaking Nations; Implies US-Australia Naval Coordination 34

Washington Dispatch: Hearst's newspapers, which advocate for a large American navy, used the stirring headline "English-Speaking Nations Unite!" on the 6th of this month, strongly advocating for friendship between the United States and Australia, implying the coordination of the navies of the two countries. This essay was also published in Australian newspapers. In response, Australian naval officer Major Gulden Stern stated, "Australia's future is inextricably linked to the Pacific. Japan will completely withdraw from the League of Nations in 1935, which is something Australia cannot ignore. Moreover, if Australia is attacked, it is impossible for the British mainland to dispatch warships. Therefore, it is necessary to jointly agree with the United States on the defense of Australia. Australia must establish a naval base on its coast, to be used for the common interests of Britain and the United States." (World News Agency)

Germany Brazenly Announces: Withdrawal from the League of Nations and Disarmament; Core Members of Disarmament Conference Meet; Simon Announces New Proposal; Mussolini Advocates Convening Conference of Four-Power Pact Nations 35

(Berlin) This afternoon, it was officially announced here that due to Geneva's opposition to Germany's demands for rearmament, Germany will withdraw from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference. German President Hindenburg has ordered the dissolution of the Reichstag, with new elections scheduled for November 11th, to gauge the people's attitude towards the government's intention to withdraw from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference. It was also stated that the President believes the new elections can obtain a clear judgment from the people, without having to submit the matter to a public referendum. (Fourteenth dispatch from the National Telegraph)

(Berlin) President Hindenburg signed an order dissolving the Reichstag, and also signed an order dissolving the parliaments of the various "Länder" (states). However, no decision has been made regarding the municipal and village councils. Chancellor Hitler is scheduled to deliver a speech at 7:00 PM tonight, broadcast nationwide via radio. Furthermore, the German government's decision to withdraw from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference will be communicated to Geneva and the governments of various countries today. (Fourteenth dispatch from Havas)

(Berlin) The German government also officially announced that it will hold a public referendum within the country on whether to approve the government's policy of withdrawing from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference. (Fourteenth dispatch from the National Telegraph)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council opened today. The German representative did not attend, but sent a letter stating that he was unable to attend, without mentioning the reason. Most of the German delegation is preparing to pack up and leave Geneva. General public opinion has expressed shock, but everyone feels that the situation is now clear and the responsibility lies with Germany. The representatives of other countries still intend to proceed with the meeting of the Disarmament General Commission on Monday. The League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference are both aiming to continue operating as usual. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

(Berlin) The announcement of Germany's withdrawal from the conference was completely unexpected by the Germans. It is widely believed that the final decision was made by President Hindenburg, as the German President could not agree to placing Germany in a position of inequality with other countries in terms of armaments. The new parliamentary elections are merely a formality, as the opposition parties have no opportunity to nominate their candidates. This election is simply to ask voters whether they support the government's actions. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

Europe is Greatly Shocked 36

(London) Europe is greatly shocked by Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference. This news was announced by German Chancellor Hitler himself at the Cabinet meeting. The reason is apparently to respond to the major powers' rejection of Germany's disarmament demands. Germany initially believed that the major powers' front had already broken, but unexpectedly, British Foreign Secretary Simon's speech at the Disarmament Conference this morning, although still moderate in tone, was very firm in its resolve. As a result, Germany realized that the major powers' front was stronger than before, and was greatly disappointed. Therefore, it made a major decision. Simon declared opposition to Germany's rearmament. US representative Davis, French representative Poncet, Italian representative Salagrana, and representatives from Greece and Czechoslovakia all agreed. At that time, it was decided to submit Simon's speech to the Disarmament General Commission meeting on Monday. However, this only indicated that Simon's proposal would receive majority support. In view of public opinion, Germany decided to withdraw from the League of Nations, rather than submit. Germany is now not only dissolving the Reichstag, so that voters can express their views on Hitler's "bomb," but also dissolving the parliaments of the various states. However, new elections for the state parliaments may not be held. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

(Paris) The French Foreign Ministry announced this afternoon after learning of Germany's withdrawal from the Disarmament Conference that Germany's decision has at least clarified the situation. The only thing to do now is to observe the reactions of the countries concerned. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

The news of Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference caused shock among the Italian people in Rome. The Italians believe that Prime Minister Mussolini has made every effort to mediate, but Germany has not reciprocated his efforts, which is very disappointing. They also feel that Germany has violated the spirit of the Four-Power Pact. The Italian Prime Minister may immediately consult with the signatory nations of the Four-Power Pact to discuss how to deal with the situation. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

(London) The British authorities have notified Prime Minister MacDonald, who is currently resting at his villa, of Germany's decision. The authorities are unwilling to make any public comments on the matter today. It is expected that a Cabinet meeting will be convened as soon as possible to discuss the current situation. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

Impact on the Far Eastern Situation 37

(London) Those who pay attention to the Far Eastern situation express the opinion that Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations will further promote Japan's plan to build warships quickly and intensify the trend of Japan and Germany collaborating to resist the League of Nations. When Reuters reporters visited Japanese Ambassador to the UK Matsudaira today, he declined to comment on Japan's attitude towards Germany's withdrawal from the Disarmament Conference and the League of Nations, saying only that the news was very important. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

US Condemns Germany as a Madhouse 38

(Geneva) An American representative, upon hearing the news of Germany's decision to break off relations with the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference, said, "What is this? Is Germany a madhouse? I never expected Germany to be so foolish and take this action. They are merely playing games with a foolish idea that can divide the major powers." (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

Core Members Meet in a Tense Atmosphere; Simon Delivers a Serious Speech 39

(Geneva) The core members of the Disarmament Conference met today in a very tense atmosphere. Many people attended the meeting. British Foreign Secretary Simon spoke, saying that the time for decorating difficult times with empty, optimistic words has passed. If the key points of the dispute are not addressed, endless discussions will not help.

Treaty Cannot Allow Rearmament 40

He believed that an agreement on a disarmament treaty cannot be established on the basis that any country is allowed to rearm. He did not want to debate whether it was reasonable or not to change the German army into a larger army with a shorter term of service and more equipment. However, at the beginning of the establishment of the treaty, there should be an agreement that the governments of various countries should not manufacture or re-equip any kind of weapons that may need to be abolished in the future.

Two Necessary Conditions for Disarmament 41

The British draft agreement unanimously adopted by the core members needs to be modified. After several discussions, it has been made clear that the term of the treaty can be extended from five years to eight years, and that a continuous procedure should be implemented during the term to achieve two necessary conditions, namely (1) disarmament special plans must be effectively completed by countries with abundant armaments, and (2) the principles of equality and security must be implemented. Politicians must deal with the reality of the instability in Europe, so the necessity of monitoring and gradual action must be clearly established. If the degree of disarmament of countries with abundant armaments is not completely sufficient, Britain cannot support this disarmament plan. The abolition of various armaments is tantamount to establishing a list of permissible weapons, which will be uniformly adopted by all countries. In this way, the different status of countries whose armaments are restricted by treaties can eventually be eliminated. In summary, this plan contains the principle that countries currently restricted by treaties should not increase their armaments, but must accept the timeline already explained. His clear wording is a clear declaration of British opinion.

France, the United States, and Italy All Speak in Favor 42

French Foreign Minister Poncet agreed with British Foreign Secretary Simon, and insisted on the necessity of managing German armaments, saying that this move is not only appropriate for the current political situation in Europe, but also requires a trial period. The purpose of the treaty is not to allow disarmed countries to rearm, but to reduce the armament standards of countries with abundant armaments to achieve equality.

US representative Davis strongly supported Simon's remarks, stating that the position adopted by the United States is that a disarmament treaty cannot be a tool for restoring armaments, but that seeking equality must be based on reducing the armaments of countries with abundant armaments, not on creating the armaments of other countries. Italian representative Salagrana also agreed with the remarks of the British Foreign Secretary.

German representative Heinbaden made a brief speech in a tense atmosphere, stating that Germany's attitude is based on two principles: first, the disarmament of countries with abundant armaments should begin immediately; second, equality between countries must be realized immediately. However, Germany is now prepared to negotiate on the amount of armaments it should have. (Fourteenth dispatch from Reuters)

(Geneva) British Foreign Secretary Simon spoke at the core committee of the Disarmament Conference, strongly opposing Germany's rearmament during the first phase of the Disarmament Treaty, and applying to other powerful armed countries to greatly reduce their armaments in the next eight years, so that Germany could be given equal rights, rather than realizing it by increasing Germany's armaments, it would be better to drastically reduce world armaments. Following this, US Ambassador Davis spoke, fully agreeing with the British government's view that the United States' position is that the Disarmament Treaty cannot be a tool for restoring armaments, but that seeking equality must be based on reducing the armaments of countries with abundant armaments, not on creating the armaments of other countries. Before Berlin declared its withdrawal from the Disarmament Conference today, US dignitaries told reporters that they believed the success or failure of the Disarmament Conference would depend on whether Germany could accept the British proposal. A spokesman for the British delegation also stated that the United States and Britain are in agreement on the entire disarmament issue, and that a resolution containing the principles stated by Simon will be submitted on Monday. In addition, it was heard that US Ambassador Davis also participated in the drafting of Simon's speech, which also shows the consistency of British and American opinions.

Three Key Points of the New British Proposal 43

The key points of British Foreign Secretary Simon's speech to the core committee are as follows:

(1) The disarmament treaty should be extended to eight years.

(2) These eight years should be divided into two phases. The first phase, perhaps four years, will standardize European armies, and Germany will guarantee not to rearm. In the second phase, the major powers should roughly follow the British draft proposal to greatly reduce armaments and allow Germany the right to equip all non-abolished weapons. (3) Establish an appropriate supervisory system to monitor the implementation of treaty obligations. Simon also pointed out that after several weapons are abolished in the second phase, the result will be a public list of weapons that are allowed to be equipped, which will be the same for all countries, without any bias. Therefore, the discriminatory status of countries whose armaments are restricted by treaties will also be finally eliminated. He also said that the principle contained in this plan is that countries currently restricted by treaties should not start to increase their armaments, but should first express their willingness to abide by the aforementioned period. The British government believes that clauses that allow immediate rearmament cannot establish a basis for agreement or treaty.

Subsequently, French Foreign Minister Poncet made a brief speech, expressing France's substantive agreement with Foreign Secretary Simon's declaration, and repeatedly stated that, in view of the actual situation in Europe, it is necessary for this conference to formulate a period for managing armaments before starting disarmament. Italian representative Sulagna only thanked Foreign Secretary Simon's declaration. Although the wording of the representatives of France and Italy was ambiguous as to whether they agreed with Foreign Secretary Simon's declaration, US officials firmly stated that the four countries of Britain, France, Italy, and the United States had completely agreed on all general principles. As for the other representatives, they all directly stated that Foreign Secretary Simon's speech had completely isolated Germany.

German Representative Insists on Two Demands 44

Since the German chief representative Nattoni has returned to his country, Reinbebein stated that he will forward Simon's proposal to Berlin for a decision, and reiterated Germany's attitude, solemnly declaring that powerful armed countries must reduce armaments and allow Germany to have an equal position, and requested

(1) To first truly and substantially reduce armaments,

(2) In order to implement the principle of equality, both the question of quality and quantity should be left for long-term discussion,

In addition, the Belgian representative made a brief statement, generally supporting Simon's declaration. The Czech Foreign Minister stated that the General Committee cannot make any progress until several key points are resolved.

Chairman Henderson then announced that Simon's report would be submitted to the General Committee on Monday. (Fourteenth dispatch from the National Telegraph)

(Berlin) German Chief Representative Nattoni rushed back to Berlin from Geneva to discuss disarmament matters with Prime Minister Hitler. After the two met today, it has been decided not to make any further concessions in Geneva. The European capitals, due to Nattoni's firm attitude in Geneva, had long expected this decision. The German representative will take back to Geneva tomorrow formal instructions announcing that Germany will no longer make concessions. Today, Berlin issued a semi-official statement, criticizing treaty proposals that would abolish the principle of equality stipulated in the Five-Power Treaty, stating that when countries with strong armaments clearly refuse to take even the slightest steps towards disarmament, certain powerful countries are trying to establish a disarmament treaty, which is contrary to the principles of international politics. The German rulers are deeply apprehensive about the means that have created a very serious situation and will endanger the disarmament work. Only by acknowledging the demands for true universal disarmament and honest equality can disarmament work be successfully completed.

British, French, and American Resolutions Withdrawn 45

The major powers had originally planned to submit a resolution based on recent talks in Paris, but this plan has now been withdrawn, probably because they knew the attitude of the German authorities. If this case is hastily submitted, it may lead to the breakdown of the Disarmament Conference and Germany's withdrawal. However, the door to continued negotiations remains open, so it is not yet the end of the road.

The United States and Italy Have Exerted Efforts to Mediate 46

It is heard that German representative Reinbaden will declare at tomorrow's core committee meeting that the disarmament of countries with strong armaments must not be delayed, and that Germany's new army should be allowed to equip appropriate weapons. The Italian representative may support this claim, as Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is now in favor of giving Germany some satisfaction in terms of armaments. German chief representative Nattoni was very angry when he departed from Geneva to return to Berlin because the three countries of Britain, France, and the United States refused to allow Germany to rearm. Therefore, when he returns to Geneva in the future, he will ask the three countries to change their policies so as not to reduce his determination. It is heard that the Italian representative has informally suggested that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini mediate. Before Nattoni hurriedly returned to Berlin, he expressed Germany's opinion that the remaining powers are now trying to force Germany to submit. It is heard that the cancellation of the formal resolution based on discussions in Paris was mainly due to the efforts of US Chief Representative Davis. Although Davis advocates that Germany should not be forced to comply with the treaty policy, he still agrees with Britain and France that Germany cannot be allowed to rearm during the first phase of the disarmament plan.

London now expects that British Foreign Secretary Simon will deliver an important speech at tomorrow's core committee meeting, outlining the process of recent talks. This talk proves that the British government holds the opinion that Germany's immediate rearmament is not permissible, and that the disarmament process should be implemented in stages. France and the United States fully agree with this opinion. During the preparatory period, the monitoring of armaments and military spending will be implemented. According to sources in London, once this measure is implemented, after a certain period of time, it can enable countries with strong armaments to make solid disarmament, and Germany can also achieve equality in the weapons that are allowed to be equipped. British Foreign Secretary Simon visited the Italian Acting Chief Representative today. According to Geneva sources, Simon had informed him of the main points of his planned declaration.

France's Attitude is Resolute 47

At the same time, in Paris, Foreign Minister Poncet had a long talk with Prime Minister Daladier. The result is unknown, but according to the Parisian newspaper Le Temps, France has reached the possible extreme in the matter of disarmament. The French government's firm attitude can be seen from this. (Thirteenth dispatch from Reuters)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Poncet returned to Paris from Geneva on the 11th and set off for Geneva again at 8:00 PM this evening. (Thirteenth dispatch from Havas)

Tense Situation in Both East and West 48

(London) The Morning Post published an article in a prominent position today, linking the Western political crisis caused by Germany's efforts to avoid unilateral disarmament with the Eastern tense situation created by Japan and Russia, declaring that many people in the League of Nations in Geneva believe that war is inevitable, and that the League of Nations is encountering the most serious crisis in history. According to the newspaper's Geneva correspondent, detailed reports on the Japan-Russia issue are now being received one after another. Most people in the League of Nations believe that war between the two countries is inevitable.

Geneva Worries About the Re-emergence of a Great War 49

It also said that Geneva is afraid that the day of a serious crisis is approaching. Although the correspondent did not explicitly say that the current situation is enough to brew a world war, he actually meant this. According to the report received in Geneva, the hope of reaching a compromise with the Germans on the armament issue has been abandoned. The tension in the Far Eastern situation also shows that a rupture between Japan and Russia is imminent. However, other newspaper correspondents in Geneva are not so pessimistic and have rarely discussed the Far Eastern issue. Most people believe that although the disarmament situation is serious, there is still hope for a compromise. A certain correspondent stated that Germany has a new informal proposal: if other countries reduce armaments, Germany can agree not to increase its military strength.

Last-Minute Efforts to Avert Crisis Through Intense Communication 50

It is also said that Berlin, Rome, and Geneva are currently engaged in intense communication via telegram in a final effort to resolve the disarmament issue. Italian leader Mussolini is attempting to persuade representatives of other countries to come to Rome to discuss the matter, but as of this morning, he has not succeeded. The General Disarmament Commission is scheduled to formally convene on Monday, but correspondents generally believe that after a brief meeting, it will adjourn to continue private talks. However, it is feared that these talks will yield little results unless the Germans make some concessions in many areas and agree not to rearm for the time being. (National Telegram, 14th)

German Government's Statement to the Nation: Same as Hitler's Declaration 51

(Berlin) The German government issued a statement to the nation, the main points of which were already seen in Hitler's personal declaration. It stated that the German government and people unanimously adopt a policy of peace and reject violence, because violence is not an appropriate means of resolving existing disputes. Germany is extremely willing to accept any genuine disarmament. Germany is prepared to destroy its last machine gun and disband its last soldier, provided that other countries do the same. The German people unanimously want to resolve difficulties through negotiations with other countries, and even with former enemy countries, they do not harbor past grudges. In order to achieve sincere relations with other countries, Germany is prepared to conclude non-aggression pacts at any time to guarantee lasting peace in Europe. However, the German people and government have the same sense of honor and feel that the necessary condition for participating in such pacts is the granting of equality to Germany. Therefore, the government and people have unanimously decided to withdraw from the Disarmament Conference and the League of Nations until Germany obtains such genuine equality. The statement concludes by asking the German people whether they support the government's policy and whether they are prepared to promote it, as an expression of public opinion. (Reuters Telegram, 14th)

Ethnic Conflict Between Jews and Arabs 102

Economic and ethnic issues are the background

A Reuters dispatch from Jerusalem on the 13th reported that conflicts between Jews and Arabs have resumed in this area. Several conflicts have occurred today, and one person was sent to the hospital due to injuries. Currently, Arab bus drivers and drivers have declared a strike after demonstrating in front of government offices against Jewish immigration.

It is reported that since Jews have been severely restricted in Germany, they have come here hoping to find a way to make a living. However, Arabs hate the return of Jews to their homeland, claiming that the current economic situation is already extremely difficult. If more immigrants are allowed to enter, it will only increase panic. Therefore, this dispute has economic and ethnic issues as its background, and it is feared that it will not be easily resolved. The police are finding it extremely difficult to prevent further conflicts, and five people have already been injured.

Contents of Technical Cooperation between the League of Nations and China—The League of Nations Sends Personnel to Assist Based on International Principles—Official Records of the League of Nations Information Department— 103

The League of Nations Information Department reported that all members of the League of Nations passed a report at the Parliamentary General Assembly in February of this year, which was later approved by the United States. It stated that "for the sake of world peace and the interests of all countries, the Chinese government should be supported so that it can realize its national aspirations." Currently, the League of Nations is acting in accordance with this report. The report mentioned that this move should expand the plan for technical meetings with the League of Nations, which began in May 1931. In June of this year, the Chinese government sent a letter to the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations, proposing the expansion of technical cooperation projects and their nature and outline. The letter strongly stated the valuable assistance that the League of Nations has already provided. The letter informed the Executive Yuan that the preliminary investigation work has now been completed. The National Government, in view of the resources it controls, has decided to start implementing its national key projects in several provinces as a model for other regions of the country. This work requires the continued efforts of all relevant parties and the coordination of various related activities. If the Executive Yuan can maintain the cooperation between the League of Nations and the National Government at this time to help its reconstruction, especially by appointing a technician to serve as an advisor to the National Government and its National Economic Council, the National Government will be deeply grateful.

The Executive Yuan then selected a committee from its members, including its acting chairman (Mexico) and representatives from China, Czechoslovakia, France, Germany, Italy, Norway, Spain, and the United Kingdom. The committee met in Paris on July 18 and elected Dr. Rajchman, Minister of Health of the League of Nations, as the aforementioned technician for a term of one year. It also stated that the principle of the cooperation plan is purely technical, fair, and non-political, with the broadest international foundation as its purpose.

The technician's responsibilities are as follows: Based on the above principles, he will serve as a liaison between the National Economic Council of China and the relevant agencies of the League of Nations, provide China with technical information from the technical organizations of the League of Nations that is beneficial to China's reconstruction, notify the Secretariat of the League of Nations of any requests for technical cooperation from the Chinese government so that they can be forwarded to the relevant technical agencies, help introduce specialized talents so that the Chinese government can take the initiative to hire them, support the activities of the League of Nations experts in China, and report the progress of his (technician's) mission to the Executive Yuan at any time, and submit a detailed report every three months. Another copy should be sent to the relevant technical agencies. The technician shall request the assistance of the Secretariat of the League of Nations to forward requests to the technical agencies when he needs to inquire about anything in the performance of his duties. Any information or reports submitted by the technician to the League of Nations shall be copied and sent to the National Economic Council of China for reference at the same time.

The committee has written to the Executive Yuan, stating that if the Chinese government raises any questions to the Executive Yuan regarding technical cooperation, the Executive Yuan must consider them, and the Executive Yuan must review the information and reports sent by the technician. The committee can provide consultations to the Executive Yuan at any time when any questions arise regarding the technician's mission. (Translated by the World Society)

An Account of the Perils of the Bandit Disaster in Luandong (Part 2)

The Dispersion of Pacified Bandits and the Conspiracy to Flee Westward 104

It has been half a month since Fu Ning was occupied by bandits. The personal desires of the bandits have been satisfied, so quite a few people have taken the opportunity to wash their hands. Moreover, since they have solved their own economic problems, most of them are unwilling to risk their lives for others. As a result, the more than 1,000 bandits who invaded Fu Ning have gradually dispersed, leaving only more than 400 people. These more than 400 bandits are stationed in the city during the day and scattered in the Zijing Mountain in the south of the city at night to prevent attacks by our security team. Until recently, the bandits planned to flee westward again, so a certain number of about 500 people mixed into Fu Ning City. As of October 9, the number of bandits in the city has increased to more than 1,000. The people of Fu Ning have suffered so much from the ravages of the bandits that they have pooled 2,000 yuan to hire a Japanese person to serve as a bodyguard. Whenever bandits come to extort or plunder, the Japanese person is responsible for resisting them. The bandits see that he is Japanese, laugh, and leave. It is now reported that the bandits in Fu Ning are planning to coordinate with the bandits on the Beidaihe coast to advance. Their plan to flee is divided into two routes. One route is to advance from the northeast of Changli. This plan has been exposed by our security team. Previously, the bandits had twice invaded Lianggezhuang. The first day was led by Rong Shan, with a total of four groups: Si Haijiao, Er Long, Er Long, and Song Ziwen. The second day, Si Haijiao was again the vanguard, carrying out the invasion. The bandits had previously learned that there were very few of our security team stationed in Lianggezhuang. However, before the bandits advanced, our reinforcements had arrived. Once they came into contact, the bandits were defeated and retreated. After being pursued, the bandits collapsed. The bandit leader Si Haijiao was also killed. The bandits on the northeast route suffered a severe blow, and their vitality was greatly damaged. As a result, there is no trace of bandits on the south bank of the Yang River. One route is to advance from the southeast, which is still in the planning stage. There are currently about 600 bandits gathered on the Beidaihe coast. They are attempting to attack along the railway line. Our security team has established a solid police force on the southeast route. It is heard that the bandits are determined to invade Changli this time and are deeply resentful of the repeated attacks by the security team. Therefore, they have been increasing the number of bandits in recent days, intending to make a final desperate effort with all their strength. Although our security team is composed of elite members, the disparity in numbers is too great. Prevention may be possible for a while, but if reinforcements are delayed, it is feared that it will be difficult to imagine. Therefore, the people of Luandong are eager for the newly formed security team to open to the east, like a great drought looking forward to rain clouds.

Refugees are Displaced Everywhere and Urgently Need Relief 105

After the bandits occupied Fu Ning, the residents of the city and suburbs all fled one after another, carrying the old and supporting the young. The destinations of the escapees are Qin Huangdao and Changli. Qin Huangdao now has more than 30,000 refugees gathered, displaced in the wilderness, a tragic sight to behold. Moreover, at this time in late autumn, they have no food or clothing and can only wait to die. Changli currently has more than 5,000 refugees, some of whom are being taken in and rescued by the Xingzhong Company, while others are also displaced in the wilderness and no one cares about them. The Beidaihe coast has about 20,000 refugees gathered. In other places such as Yu Guan Town, the number of refugees is countless. Although it is now the time for the war zone emergency relief team to provide relief, it cannot save these refugees from their dire situation. Moreover, the refugees' family property has long been looted by the bandits, and their future livelihoods have been cut off. To talk about relief, it is necessary to find fundamental solutions for them. Otherwise, if it is delayed until the middle of winter, if the refugees are forced into detours due to livelihood pressures, it will affect the overall situation in Luandong, which is no small matter.

Dou Xizhe is Willing to Live and Die with Changli 106

Dou Xizhe, the commander of the Hebei Provincial Security Corps, leads 2,000 strong men to support the precarious situation in Luandong. Being able to protect Changli today is truly a testament to his hard work. The reporter visited Dou several times in Changli. Every time we talked, Dou was so excited that he shed tears. According to Dou, "The security team currently has only more than 2,000 people, distributed in various places in Luandong. The battle of Fu Ning was actually forced to retreat due to the constraints of the rear. I have no regrets in my heart for the elders of Luandong. Now that Fu Ning is no longer defended, the relationship with Changli is not comparable to Fu Ning. Changli is the throat of Yutian, Lulong, and Leting counties. I am determined to deal with everything with all my strength. As for my personal life and death, I have long put it aside. I am willing to live and die with Changli City. Moreover, I will never be forced by any threats. My subordinates have also made vows of 'either bandits or me' and 'either me or no bandits.' Now that Changli is surrounded by bandits, I am confident that with the well-trained police force, dealing with the rabble of bandits, even if the number of bandits is several times greater than ours, it will not be difficult to defeat them. I originally intended to take advantage of the westward fleeing of the bandits and launch a head-on attack until Fu Ning was recovered. However, Changli's relationship is important. If a large force enters Fu Ning, and the rear of Changli is scattered in strength and re-entered by the bandits, the overall situation in Luandong will be impossible to clean up. Therefore, I am currently devoting all my efforts to protecting Changli, and will plan to recover Fu Ning after the reinforcements arrive. Moreover, solid defensive works have been set up on the east, south, and north sides of the suburbs of Changli. If the bandits come to invade, there are ways to deal with them. The current situation in Luandong is quite complicated. The bandit disaster in Luandong is rampant, and there are certain constraints in western Luandong, placing me in a state of siege on all sides, which is quite difficult. However, since I am responsible for defending the territory, I can only swallow my tears and do my best. As for the merits and demerits, I can only leave it to fate." (10th)

Chairman Chiang's National Day Commemorative Speech

Only by Cultivating a Spirit of Propriety, Righteousness, Integrity, and Shame Can the Suppression of Bandits and Resistance Against Japan Not Become a Problem 107

A Nanjing dispatch reported that the Jiangxi Provincial National Day Commemorative Party and government agencies held a joint meeting. The attendees included all members of the Provincial Party Department, all members of the Provincial Government, officers above the rank of section chief of the headquarters, and more than 2,000 representatives from various agencies, groups, and schools, who gathered in the auditorium of the Provincial Party Department. The Provincial Government Guard was responsible for guarding the surrounding area. At 10:10 AM, Chairman Chiang also arrived. Chairman Xiong of the Provincial Government and Director He of the headquarters followed behind. After the meeting and salute were held as usual, Chiang delivered a speech, which is recorded as follows:

"Fellow comrades, today is the National Day of the Republic of China in the 22nd year. It has been 22 years since the Republic of China. Our Premier and martyrs sacrificed themselves for the revolution, for the creation of the Republic of China, and for the realization of our party's doctrine. And later, in the suppression of traitors and bandits, many comrades of our party also sacrificed their lives and the production of all the people. Especially the turmoil of bandits in Jiangxi made it impossible for the people to live and work in peace. Our Premier and martyrs in heaven must be uneasy, and the comrades of our party and the military and political personnel in office should feel very uneasy. Regarding the National Day commemoration, in foreign countries, it is a grand celebration day. It is truly a national celebration and a great honor. But although our Republic of China has grown to 22 years old, it is like a person. The Premier is so old and should have the ability to be self-reliant and self-defensive and not allow foreign insults. But now there is internal turmoil from bandits and external aggression from imperialists. We in-service personnel, on this National Day, looking back at the difficulty of the Premier's creation of the Republic of China and the sacrifices of the martyrs who created the Republic of China, only feel frightened and infinitely ashamed. We are sorry for the Premier and the martyrs in heaven. My personal feelings are like this, and I believe everyone's feelings are the same. Today, I have a few opinions to offer to everyone. A country must have a soul in order to survive, be sound, and stable. What is a soul? For example, if a person's body grows up but has no soul, he will only become a clay sculpture or wooden puppet. Today's China is like this. Although it has grown into a big man, is strong, independent, and has all kinds of skills, intelligence, and learning, it only lacks a soul. In the 22 years since the founding of the Republic of China, from 15 to 20 years, there has been a lot of glorious history, but after that, it has been in tragedy, pain, and danger every day. Now it is even more dangerous. The Premier and the martyrs entrusted the difficult-to-create Republic of China to us. We comrades who have died and not yet died cannot continue to promote and develop it in order to comfort the souls of the Premier and the martyrs in heaven. We ask ourselves, can we not be ashamed? In the future, if we want to continue to promote and develop the glorious history of the martyrs, we must first enrich the soul of the country. What is the soul of China? It is the Three Principles of the People. What is the important part of the Three Principles of the People? It is the eight characters "loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace" that the Premier said. It should be known that China has reached the 22nd year and is a good youth. He should be able to inherit the cause of his parents and ancestors. Now, not only can he not be independent, but he is also oppressed by foreign insults. The territory is being eroded day by day, and the people are suffering every day. The future is so dangerous. What is the reason? Because although people have grown up and have all kinds of skills, intelligence, and learning, they lack loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace. This is a big problem. The reason why China has become what it is now is because it is only hanging a sign of the Republic of China without obtaining the spirit of the Republic of China. If we want to obtain the spirit of the Republic of China, we must do the eight characters of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace that the Premier said. Now, I will change the eight characters into four characters, which are propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. It should be known that a nation cannot be established without morality. The comrades of our party and all the personnel in office have more than enough ability, intelligence, talent, and learning compared with foreigners. What is lacking is the four characters of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. All in-service personnel are responsible for the rise and fall of the nation. If we want to revitalize China and comfort the souls of the Premier and the martyrs in heaven, we must start with the four characters of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame in today's National Day commemoration, set an example for the people, and be a model for the people. If all the in-service personnel cannot achieve propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, then China will only sink forever and will not stop until it is destroyed. I hope everyone will abide by this righteousness and lay the foundation for revitalizing China and consolidating the nation. Talking about the four characters of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame is not something that can be done by talking about it, nor can it be done by writing a few sentences. It must be done in practice. If we want to do it in practice, we must understand what propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are. As far as propriety is concerned, what is propriety? The ancients said, "If a person has no propriety, he cannot be a human being." From this, we can see the importance of propriety. In other words, if a country has no propriety, it cannot become a country. The national difficulties, bandit disasters, and people's suffering in China today can mostly be blamed on not knowing propriety. For example, during the Premier's memorial week, we must bow three times and salute the national flag and party flag. What does this mean? Does everyone know? If you don't know, then bowing three times at random is meaningless. If there is no meaning, there is no feeling. Today, I will explain it. I hope everyone will go back and explain it to those who have not been here to make it universal, especially those in the education sector. Elementary school teachers should be especially clear. On the first day of school, we must tell the students that the national flag and party flag are where the souls of the Premier and the martyrs are entrusted. We salute the party flag and national flag because there are souls of martyrs on them, not random salutes. Not only must we salute, but we must also protect and cherish them. Foreign countries regard the national flag as a representative of the country. If someone insults his national flag, he is insulting his entire country. Looking back at our countrymen, do we have such feelings? We hang the national flag casually and messily without respect, love, or care. If we do not respect and love the national flag, we do not know how to respect and love the country. From now on, everyone must know the importance of the national flag. If you don't know, you are not worthy to be a citizen of the Republic of China, especially elementary school teachers. We must explain it to the students so that we don't always create students who don't love the country or the party. Of course, we won't have any feelings about any commemoration. How can the country be sound? If we can make everyone understand the meaning of saluting the national flag and party flag, then we will know how to cherish, protect, and respect them and generate feelings for the nation and the country. We won't bow casually anymore. The party flag has two meanings: the blue sky and white sun. The national flag has three meanings: the blue sky, white sun, and red earth. This is what everyone knows. Why does the national flag have three meanings? This is also what everyone should know, because it is the representative of our country. We make a living under it. If there is no national flag, everyone will be slaves of a conquered nation. The two colors of the national flag are blue sky, white sun, and red earth. The red is blood, the blood that the martyrs sacrificed to create the revolution, establish the Republic of China, and sacrifice for the country and the people. That is why their souls are entrusted on it. The blue sky and white sun are twelve rays of light. The twelve rays of light represent the twelve hours of the day: Zi, Chou, Yin, Mao, Chen, Si, Wu, Wei, Shen, You, Xu, Hai. It means that it is bright and upright, causing people to think about it for thousands of years. The comrades of our party take the sacrifice of themselves to save the country and the people as their purpose, and only then can they live up to the four words of uprightness and brightness. Blue represents the sky. The sky is supreme. Only the nature of our party is for the entire nation and country, selfless, and supreme. White means purity and flawless, which means that our revolutionary comrades must have a pure heart and spirit and morality, just like a piece of jade, pure and flawless. This is also what only the comrades of our party can afford. In the future, all of you, especially the in-service government and military personnel, must have a pure heart, noble character, and ambition to sacrifice for the country and the people. You must sprinkle your blood on the national flag and entrust your souls on the national flag and party flag. In today's National Day, saluting the Premier's portrait and the party and national flags has such a meaning. Propriety must be in accordance with righteousness. Propriety without righteousness cannot be propriety. Therefore, propriety cannot be done casually and cannot be easily talked about. Everyone must pay attention to this so that the country can be stable. If we want to have a sound country, we must start with elementary school students and continue until death. If we want to suppress bandits and resist foreign insults, we cannot just rely on the army. We must rely on the four characters of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Today, in commemorating the National Day, we should use propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame to lay the foundation of the country. We should start with Jiangxi. If Jiangxi is secured, then we can eliminate the bandits. If the bandits are eliminated, then we can stabilize the people's hearts. If the people's hearts are stabilized, then the Republic of China can be consolidated. If you can set an example and popularize it among your friends and comrades to cultivate a spirit of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, then not only can the bandits be completely eliminated, but I also believe that we can be restored to a country of propriety and righteousness. Then, if we promote and popularize it throughout China as a country of propriety and righteousness, then suppressing bandits and resisting Japan will not become a problem. Finally, I hope that everyone will start with the Premier and the party and national flags in today's National Day commemoration, starting with yourselves and then others, to revitalize China and comfort the souls of the Premier and the martyrs in heaven. At the same time, I encourage everyone to achieve their own great cause."

After Chiang finished his speech, he shouted slogans: (1) The National Day commemoration is a commemoration of our party's creation of the Republic of China. (2) To commemorate the National Day, we must eliminate the bandits. (3) To commemorate the National Day, we must work hard to resist Japan. (4) Support the government, implement unity, and ensure peace and unification. (5) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang. (6) Long live the Three Principles of the People. (7) Long live the Republic of China. After shouting, he took photos in the garden outside the hall. First, Chairman Chiang took photos alone, and then all the attendees took photos together. The meeting adjourned at about 12:00 noon. (Datong Society)

Jiangsu People Request New Provincial Government: Financial Planning to Streamline, Rural Areas Urgently Need Relief 108

Zhang Yilin and thirteen others from Jiangsu sent a telegram to the new Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman Chen Guofu and others on the 13th: "To Chairman Chen, Director Gu of the Civil Affairs Department, and Director Zhao of the Finance Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government in Zhenjiang. We have heard about your appointment and are all very excited. We believe that your new plans will satisfy the public's expectations and reach the highest level of governance. Jiangsu Province has suffered from repeated floods, war disasters, and low grain prices that have harmed farmers. Farmers work hard all year round but cannot get enough to eat. Women seek employment in cities, and strong men leave their villages. Land is barren and neglected, and the people are deeply impoverished. We know that you have already considered how to cultivate and comfort them, and we don't need to worry too much. However, we want to say that the provincial treasury is extremely depleted, and there are all kinds of construction projects. There is no inexhaustible source, so we must first reduce unnecessary expenses. We must plan and discuss with the public in a comprehensive manner so that donations can be used for urgent needs, and both can be achieved. We hope that the wise and bright officials will listen to good advice and cultivate the national foundation, soothe the people's breath, and always remember the mulberry tree's suffering, and also adopt the words of the common people. We ask that you distinguish between how to help rural areas, develop production, and abolish policies that severely burden the people, so that your virtuous voice will be spread and we will see thunderous cheers. We respectfully offer our humble opinions and hope that you will accept them. We are extremely fortunate. Zhang Yilin, Fei Shuwei, Jin Tianhe, Zeng Pu, Zhao Yichen, Ding Huaiqing, Qian Ding, Shen Shaozeng kowtow. Zhang Yilin and others also sent a telegram to former Chairman Gu Zhutong and others: "To Chairman Gu of the Zhenjiang Provincial Government, Director Zhao of the Civil Affairs Department, and Director Shu of the Finance Department. When you took over the Jiangsu government, it was after floods and war disasters. The provincial treasury was extremely depleted, and the rural areas were on the verge of bankruptcy. Fortunately, you were wise and understood the people's concerns. Therefore, although the two proposals on grain transport reduction, special characteristics, permanent tenancy, and taxation were once considered, they were eventually exempted or postponed due to public opinion. The people all understand that the provincial government above is considering the national economy and below is relieving the people's breath, with the painstaking efforts of considering both, and not exploiting the people for political purposes. Now that we hear that you are leaving Jiangsu, our love and respect are deep. There is no way to keep you, and we are frightened and worried that the previous achievements will not be completed and that there will be changes in the future. Therefore, we send a telegram again, begging you to specially transfer the archives of the two proposals so that we can obtain a deep and solid guarantee and leave a glimmer of hope for the revival of rural areas. We are extremely fortunate. Zhang Yilin, Fei Shuwei, Jin Tianhe, Zeng Pu, Zhao Yichen kowtow."

Li Zongren Returns to Guangxi to Rectify Military and Political Affairs; Reduces the Armies in the Whole Province; Trains Local Armed Forces; Establishes Seven Air Force Districts 109

Guangzhou Dispatch: After assuming the position of committee member of the Southwest Political Affairs Council, Li Zongren, commander-in-chief of the Fourth Army Group of Guangxi, spent most of his time in Guangdong. Recently, to discuss the current situation and reorganize the military and political affairs of Guangxi Province, he returned to Guangxi from Guangdong on the morning of October 3. Accompanying him were his wife, Guo Dejie, and over twenty adjutants and guards. Before leaving, he requested a one-month leave from the Southwest Political Affairs Council, promising to return to Guangdong as soon as the military and political affairs of Guangxi Province were settled. On the afternoon of the 3rd, Li arrived at Hekou by Guangsan train and transferred by steamer to Wu. He arrived in Wuzhou at 8 a.m. on the 4th. Bai Chongxi, who was on an inspection tour to Xunzhou, went to Wuzhou to greet Li upon hearing of his arrival. Bai and Li stayed in Wuzhou for one night. On the 5th, they went west together and arrived in Nanning on the afternoon of the 6th. It is reported that Li's most important task this time is to discuss the current situation with Bai Chongxi and the generals of Guangxi Province. He will also inspect the troops of Guangxi Province and inspect the defenses of various places. There will also be some reforms in military and political affairs. A military conference may be held in Yong. It was rumored a few days ago that the troops of Guangxi Province were being reorganized. According to Bai Chongxi's opinion, it is planned to reorganize the entire Guangxi military strength into sixteen regiments, abolish the military adjustment, and change to using the division as a unit. Guangxi will be temporarily reorganized into five divisions, each division commanding three regiments and one artillery regiment. Each division and regimental headquarters will have special troops such as special service companies and platoons. The entire Guangxi will be reorganized into approximately twenty-two regiments. As for the militia in various counties, they have been actively trained. Those who have been trained to maturity have about 150,000 militias or more. Those who have been organized into standing teams are about 240 teams, with more than 120 militiamen in each team, totaling about 30,000 people. These militias are all under the command of the county government. Because they are well-trained, regardless of whether they are formal defense forces, Li and Bai believe that this militia has a certain scale and the local self-defense force is sufficient. Therefore, the active army is temporarily reduced to save military expenses. At the same time, the surplus military expenses will be used to expand the air force. The Guangxi Air Force is also quite impressive. At the aviation memorial meeting held in Guangdong Province a few days ago, Guangxi Province also had ten planes participating in the flight to Guangdong. Currently, in addition to raising funds to purchase airplanes, the training of flight personnel is being stepped up and the overall plan for the Guangxi Air Force is being implemented, designating seven locations, including Nanning, Longzhou, Bose, Guilin, Yulin, Hexian, and Wuzhou, as air force districts in the province, with Liuzhou as the air force headquarters. Each air force district has a flying field to achieve the effect of liaison and command. Some of the above-mentioned matters have already been carried out, and some are still awaiting planning. Therefore, Li Zongren's return to Guangxi this time is for planning and preparation. (October 9)

Two Homicides Occur in the Fourth District 116

Liu Chunlan, director of the 9th branch of the Public Security Bureau, received a secret report on the evening of the day before yesterday at 11 p.m. saying that someone in the Bai Xun Nunnery in Daishang Village, Fourth District, was gathering people for gambling under the guise of storytelling. Please investigate and arrest them. Director Liu immediately led police officers to surround the nunnery and ordered the police officers to knock on the door to enter and arrest the gamblers. At that time, a villager, Gu Zhongxiang, took the opportunity to escape from the back door into the river. Unexpectedly, he did not know how to swim, and he floated and sank in the water. Director Liu had already arrested seven gamblers and sent them to the 9th branch for interrogation. After the police officers left, the villagers gathered to rescue him. However, Gu died of suffocation due to excessive water absorption. The next morning, Gu's wife, Ms. Lu, heard the news and rushed to the scene, wailing while holding the body. At the same time, villager Wu Genshou also drowned in the river at the same place. Zhu, the district chief of the district, instructed the head of the Tuanding, Miao Yugui, to report to the county court yesterday (the 14th) and request that someone be sent for an autopsy. The prosecutor, Ren, led the coroner, Wang, to the scene for an autopsy and determined that he had fallen into the river and died. The family of the deceased was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial and await verification. In addition, Zhang Renjin, a villager in Xiaxiaoqiao, Liuliutu, Jingyun City, Second District of the county, 32 years old, was a bowl repairer. On the 26th of last month, Zhang went out again with his burden. On the evening of the 11th of this month, in Dazhuzhuang, Wuwujiu Tu, in the same district, he was suddenly beaten to death by villagers Zhu Quangen and others. Afterwards, the body was moved to the side of the Huasifang tomb beside the railway in Liuliuliu Tu in the same district. Shao Yueji, the head of the Tu, discovered it the day before yesterday and immediately reported it to the county court. Prosecutor Shen led officials to the countryside for an autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the deceased had a fatal wound on the back of his head caused by a wooden object, and there were rope marks on both hands. He had been beaten to death before his death. Because no family members were found, Tu Zheng was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial. Yesterday morning (the 14th), the deceased's wife, Zhang Wu, heard the news and came to the city, requesting the prosecutor's office to arrest the murderer and bring him to justice.

Shanghai Teenager Commits Suicide in Wuxi 117

At about 10 a.m. on the 11th of this month, a single traveler arrived at the Wuxi Hotel under the Gonglian Bridge in this city, creating the name Shen Chen, a native of Shanghai, 24 years old, wearing a Zhongshan style student uniform and carrying a small leather bag. He booked room 72 on the third floor. He did not go out that day. At about 9 p.m., he turned off the lights and went to bed. He got up at 8 a.m. the next morning and went out once. At 2 p.m., he returned to his room and asked the tea room for ink, paper, and writing materials, and then swallowed sleeping pills to commit suicide. At about 4 p.m. yesterday, the medicine took effect. Yuan Fupei, the tea room attendant, heard the groans, entered the room, and saw that his face was pale. He asked him, but he did not answer. He knew that he had taken poison. He then found a bottle of sleeping pills and four suicide notes on the table, and a photo of a girl about 18 or 19 years old in a small leather bag, with the words "No. 61, First Hostel, North Station" and "Lingzeng Memorial" written on the back. He immediately reported it to the manager, Wu Weichu, and reported it to the Second Branch, sending Shen Chen to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The doctor at the hospital washed his stomach and gave him an injection, and he was revived. After repeated inquiries by Tang, the patrol chief of the Second Branch, the teenager's reason for suicide was said to be caused by a bad environment, and he absolutely denied that it was for love.

Labor Unrest in the Barber Industry Expands 118

The barber industry in this city consists of small shops with a shortage of capital. Recently, due to the sluggish business, price reductions have been implemented to attract customers, which has affected the income of the shop assistants. Strikes have occurred in barber shops around Zhoushanbang. Later, members of the county party department, together with members of the industry association, went to various places to order the removal of the price reduction notices. The police of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau arrested Sha Laoer, the owner of Shanrongxuan, and Liu Dabang of Meihua Store, who were the first to reduce prices. They were released on bail. After being released from the bureau, Sha and Liu believed that the small shops mainly served farmers and workers and were affected by the large shops. The price reduction of the small shops was actually due to the problem of eating and was forced by the environment. The shop assistants were quite dissatisfied. At 2 p.m. on the day before yesterday, they sent representatives holding red flags to notify the barber shops inside and outside the city to continue the strike. At about 8 p.m., more than 100 striking workers flocked to the Meirongxuan and Meihua barber shops to question them. In case of disagreement, they took action and destroyed all the shop's belongings. Later, the police of the Second Branch arrested thirteen people, including Ju Changxing, Zhang Yongbao, Qian Baohua, and Yunlong, who had caused the incident, and brought them to the bureau along with Sha Laoer and Liu Dabang. The acting director of the branch, Cheng, held a court session for preliminary interrogation. Ju Changxing directly admitted to the destruction. Director Cheng, after hearing the confession, transferred all the arrested criminals to the headquarters for interrogation at 10 a.m. yesterday (the 14th). At the same time, the Inspection Department of the County Public Security Bureau and the Police Brigade immediately dispatched patrol teams to assist the Second Branch in maintaining order on the streets to prevent accidents. It is unknown how the strike will be resolved.

What Was Heard After the Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits 120

The situation of the fierce battle between the police and bandits in the Shenxiangdang, Jiashan County, was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It has been learned that the bandit gang is the Pudong Gang, which has always been rampant and has committed numerous crimes in the villages along the borders of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. This time, they robbed the Jiashan Tiande Medicine Shop and the boats carrying rice, and the peasant Yu was learned by Gao Zengzhi, the leader of the Jiadiao Security Corps Base Team, who led 18 team members and militiamen to suppress them. Unexpectedly, the bandits learned of the news and ambushed in the bamboo forest behind Zhoujiacao Village in the north of Shenxiangdang and launched a surprise attack, resulting in the complete annihilation of the Security Corps, resulting in an unprecedented tragedy. It is estimated that Lu Zijia, Hu Changfa, Shen Ziren, Chen Zhiwen, Ma Bingsheng, etc. died, and the rest were seriously injured and in critical condition. All the guns and boats were lost, and more than 1,600 bullets were lost. The county Security Corps and the Water and Land Police Brigade, led by Huang Ribin, the captain of the Yiwei warship, advanced to suppress them and are currently engaged in fierce battles near Dajinze. The families of the deceased knelt before the district regiment leader and the police brigade commander, begging for redress with cries of sorrow, which made those who heard it shed tears. Some even witnessed the bodies with bullet marks all over them, and they cried and jumped into the river to seek death. Moreover, they are all extremely poor and cannot afford coffins. As for Hu Changfa, he was originally from Anhui, and he was alone, which made the situation even more bleak and unspeakable. The county magistrate, Huang, urgently telegraphed the Security Department to implement condolences. The provincial authorities were very concerned after receiving the report of the tragedy and discussed suppression day and night in order to eliminate them in one fell swoop. Otherwise, the bandits would become more daring and the flames of robbery would become more intense, and the northwestern regions would become bandit areas.

Goods Marked with Country of Origin; Counterfeit Goods Will Be Severely Punished by the Government 126

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the silk and satin industry, cotton cloth industry, and mercerized cotton velvet industry and other associations yesterday, stating: "To whom it may concern, on the 13th of this month, we received an order from the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, No. 16070, stating: "We have approved the Nanjing Municipal Government's Consultation No. 7467, according to Wang Zhichong, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau of this city, stating: "I have secretly investigated that the National Goods Consumption Committee of this government has been organized and established. However, the various silk and cloth shops always sell national goods and non-national goods together, which is confusing. I hereby order that the persons in charge of the relevant trade associations be summoned immediately to discuss and determine the method of marking national goods and non-national goods so that they can be distinguished and the citizens can avoid making mistakes. This was determined at 2:30 p.m. on August 26 to summon the persons in charge of the silk, cloth, satin, and factory cloth trade associations to discuss and decide on three principles: 1. Each silk and cloth shop should mark national goods and non-national goods with labels. Larger ones may set up a special department to sell national goods separately. 2. If each silk and cloth shop sells non-national goods as national goods, the government will severely punish them. 3. The detailed methods of items 1 and 2 will be formulated and promulgated by the Social Affairs Bureau. The Director of the Agriculture, Industry, and Commerce Section of this Bureau has drafted seven rules for marking goods in silk and cloth shops in Nanjing with the General Secretary of the National Goods Consumption Committee of this government. Is this feasible? I hereby submit a document for your review and approval. This is for the public convenience, etc. According to this, after reviewing the proposed rules, there is nothing inappropriate. In addition to announcing and ordering the implementation of the rules, I will copy the rules and send them to you for your reference and record, and I hope to see a reply, etc. After receiving the order, it was found that the silk shops displayed Chinese and foreign goods in a mixed manner, so that those who wanted to purchase national goods could not distinguish them, which had a great impact on promoting national goods and promoting production and sales. The Municipal Government revised the rules and notified the silk and cloth shops to follow them, displaying the goods sold, which were manufactured in a certain country, separately, or adding labels so that purchasers would know the difference and choose them, which was very beneficial to the promotion of national products. Before approving the consultation, in addition to the above rules being approved for record, a copy of the rules should be inspected and copied, and you should refer to them for handling and report as necessary, etc." According to this, it is urgent to send the marking rules and a provisional standard for national goods to the relevant associations for compliance, transfer orders, and reports, etc., and I deeply hope to receive your reply. The attachment is a copy of the rules for marking goods in silk and cloth shops in Nanjing and a provisional standard for Chinese national goods.

Local Daily Coal Declines, Domestic Coal Sales Gradually Increase; Coal Control Association Has Not Yet Been Implemented 127

A reporter from the Daba newspaper inquired about the current situation of domestic coal and Japanese coal in Shanghai from the coal industry. It was learned that the amount of Japanese coal recently transported and sold in this city has decreased by 70% compared to the past. The sales of domestic coal have therefore gradually developed. After the implementation of the new tariff, the tax rate for imported coal has increased by more than four yuan per ton compared to the past, so Japanese coal can no longer compete with domestic coal. Although there are still a few sales, they are entirely for Japanese merchants to purchase and use for themselves, so Japanese coal is almost extinct in the market. As for the Coal Control Association proposed by the National Economic Commission, there is currently no action in the coal industry, and the Economic Commission has not yet contacted the coal industry. It may wait until the Cotton and Silk Control Associations are established before proceeding. It is also impossible to say.

Sa Zhenbing's Remarks: This Time I Come to Specially Prepare for the Zhenwu of Fujian Province; I Deeply Hope for the Support of the Government and All Circles 128

The Minyan newspaper reported that after the naval veteran Sa Zhenbing arrived in Shanghai, he was busy contacting matters related to the disaster relief in Fujian, and he still had contacts with foreign treasure and relatives and friends here. Yesterday, a reporter from the Minyan newspaper specially visited Mr. Sa's residence, and he was received and informed of the mission and the progress of disaster relief in detail. A record is as follows: "I have been living in my hometown for many years and have long forgotten about politics. This time I came to discuss the disaster relief in Fujian with various parties, and the time of my stay will be very short. I feel guilty that I have not been able to visit all my old friends here and friends from various countries. Fujian Province has suffered from natural disasters and man-made disasters in recent years, and the beautiful mountains and rivers are full of scars. What I have heard and seen makes me feel sad, and many of my fellow villagers also blame me for the disaster relief affairs. Thinking of Fujian as my hometown, if it is beneficial to my hometown, how can I shirk my responsibility? Therefore, I do not hesitate to take on this task rashly. Fortunately, my body is still strong. For several years, I have been running around in remote and poor villages day and night. Fortunately, I have not been attacked by diseases or trapped by bandits. After a long time of practice, I feel that the life in the countryside is very interesting. When I was releasing disaster relief in Longyan, it was only ten miles away from the bandit area, and the thieves also knew that I was foolish and did not want to harm me. I also advised the militia to cultivate their own strength and guide them to build earthen forts and gun towers. During the conversation, Mr. Sa also showed photos and said that many counties in northwestern Fujian have deep mountains and poor valleys and that he had heard that there were sheep intestines trails that people had not been through and that horses could not pass through. Fortunately, I was from the navy and had been through wind and frost for a long time. Although I was old, my experience was still there. I often supervised the regiment soldiers and walked up the mountains. One day, I encountered heavy rain and flash floods, and the water could submerge my shins. Fortunately, the weather cleared up soon, and I was safe and sound. As for enduring freezing and hunger, it has been my daily life in recent years, and I dare not say that it is hard. Recently, I was mistakenly the director of the Changle County disaster relief, and I have a lot of debts besides the government's appropriation and Mr. Hu Wenhu's donation of 5,000 yuan, and I still need the assistance of generous charities from all parties. As for the various counties in northern Fujian, which have recently suffered from the Red Disaster, the severity of the disaster and the extent of the disaster area are not known to the outside world. I hope that the government authorities and people from all walks of life will give them sympathy and assistance. I am old and wish to engage in this matter."
