Letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council 132

To the Esteemed Council,

It has come to our attention that the Shanghai Telephone Company increased its prices last year, disregarding the impact of the January 28th Incident, and retroactively applied the increase, violating legal precedents. Your council, being in charge, failed in your responsibility to advise and prevent this, leading to its approval, creating a significant error, and leaving a blemish. A year has passed, and the company naturally seizes this opportunity to aggressively advance its interests, disregarding contracts and agreements. It imposes unforeseen responsibilities on Mr. An Sheng, while seeking to fully recoup its own miscalculations from users. This association firmly believes that your council will certainly reject the company's current request for a price increase. We earnestly hope that your council will carefully consider the correspondence between the First District Branch of the Shanghai Citizens' United Association and the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association regarding this matter, as published in the newspapers. What deserves your council's deepest reflection is how the Municipal Council, in managing public utilities, should protect taxpayers, ensuring they can use these services at affordable prices. However, the reality does not align with this principle. In the case of tap water, the council agreed to the water company's amendments to the contract, allowing it to raise prices at will, causing taxpayers to lose significant amounts of money. In the case of electricity, the council permitted price increases due to rising coal prices, but failed to order price reductions when coal prices fell. The same applies to trams and public buses. It is widely known that the authorities disregard the interests of taxpayers. The Shanghai Telephone Company, taking advantage of this weakness, naturally dares to raise prices repeatedly and attempt to disregard contracts. The written agreement of the thirtieth year of the Republic of China can be ignored. In short, for all contractual provisions beneficial to taxpayers, the Municipal Council makes every effort to disregard public opinion. This matter concerns the sanctity of public utilities and contractual agreements. We, therefore, respectfully request your council to no longer be misled by the company, lest those you represent suffer further damage.

Respectfully submitted to the Public Concession Municipal Council,

The First District Citizens' United Association of Shanghai Special District,

China Merchants Bureau's Request for Appropriation of Funds Approved, Borrowing from Shanghai Banking Syndicate to Repay HSBC Loan of 10 Million, Using Five Warehouse Deeds as Guarantee 136

The China Merchants Bureau mortgaged five warehouse deeds to HSBC Bank for a substantial loan, initially for five million taels, followed by an additional one million taels. Including interest, the total amount exceeded ten million yuan. This time, HSBC is

Demanding Repayment of the Mortgage Loan 137

and has ordered the Bureau to repay the loan within a specified period, or it will seize control of the warehouses. General Manager of the Bureau, Liu Hongsheng, facing urgent demands from HSBC, found it difficult to delay further. On September 18th, he presented the matter to the Board of Directors. After discussion, the Board members collectively agreed that the Bureau could not raise such a large sum of money in the short term. The petition was submitted to the Ministry of Communications through the Board of Directors and has recently received

Approval from the Ministry 138

Regarding the Bureau's request to allocate 15 million yuan as a state-owned fund, the Ministry has approved the request in principle. However, the central government is currently facing economic difficulties and cannot immediately allocate such a large sum of money. As the HSBC mortgage loan cannot be extended, the Ministry instructed General Manager Liu to find a way to borrow 15 million yuan from the Shanghai banking community and to transfer the five warehouse

Deeds as Collateral 139

to the banking community as security for the new loan. Once the central government's economic situation improves, it will then allocate funds to redeem the warehouses. Upon receipt of the Ministry's approval in Shanghai, the government has, in principle, approved the request to issue funds, but is unable to allocate them due to financial constraints. General Manager Liu is preparing to comply with the Ministry's instructions and seek a fund loan of 15 million yuan from national banks in Shanghai. He will then use the five warehouse deeds retrieved from HSBC

As Collateral 140

For this loan, 10 million yuan will be used to repay HSBC and other miscellaneous loans, and the remaining funds will be used to develop the shipping industry. It is reported that Liu has recently begun negotiations with various banks in the city for this loan. Most banks are willing to provide the loan, but there are still some points for discussion regarding the loan terms. On the whole, success is expected.

After the Arrest of Korean Resident Lee Seong-gu, Kong Kaiping was Summoned. Naturalized Korean Citizens are in Danger, Hoping for Assistance from the Chinese Government 141

According to the Fuxing Society, Saeki, Chief of the Criminal Section of the Japanese Consulate, Fujii, Chief of Police, Goto, Chief of Patrol, and twelve others, in conjunction with the French police, arrested Korean resident Lee Seong-gu on the 12th, believing that he was strongly suspected of involvement in the two grenade-throwing incidents at the Japanese Consulate. On the afternoon of the 13th, Korean resident Kong Kaiping, owner of the Baekje Pharmacy at 406 Avenue Joffre, at the intersection of Rue Lubin in the French Concession, was also summoned by the Japanese Consulate and imprisoned. A reporter from the Fuxing Society inquired about the details yesterday. The details are as follows:

Lee's Arrest Location 142

Lee Seong-gu was arrested on the morning of the 12th. At that time, Lee was going to the Baekje Pharmacy. Before Lee arrived, two cars were parked near the French barracks at the corner of Avenue Joffre and Rue Dupanloup. When Lee Duofu entered the Baekje Pharmacy, a Chinese man followed him in and briefly examined Lee, then bought a rubber tube and left. While Lee was paying, another Chinese man, followed by nine Japanese, two French police officers, and three Chinese police officers, broke into the Baekje Pharmacy, surrounded Lee, and immediately arrested him, put him in a waiting car, and drove to the French police station, which extradited him to the Japanese Consulate.

Kong's Surrender 143

After Lee was arrested, the Japanese Consulate determined that the Baekje Pharmacy was a communication center for Korean residents, and then notified the French police station to send criminal police to arrest Kong. Coincidentally, Kong was out. Afterwards, knowing that it was inevitable, Kong resolutely surrendered himself to the Japanese Consulate and was detained for interrogation. As of 6:00 PM yesterday, there was still no news. In addition to running the Baekje Pharmacy, Kong also runs the International Year Hong Company (intersection of Beijing Road and Sichuan Road) and is a well-known businessman among Korean residents. The Japanese Consulate believes that Kong is suspected of communication, and claims that Park Chang-se, the leader of the Korean Revolutionary Party's special forces, often visits the Baekje Pharmacy.

Lee's Wife Prevented from Visiting 144

Lee Seong-gu, also known as Lee Soo-bong, is from Seoncheon County, Pyeonganbuk-do, Korea. He is 37 years old and married Ms. Kim Yun-ju just before May. Kim is 21 years old, beautiful, and from Pyeongwon, Korea. She graduated from the local girls' high school and speaks English. Since Lee's arrest, Jin has been running around for two days and two nights without sleep. Yesterday afternoon, she told the Fuxing Society reporter that Lee became a Chinese citizen on June 23, 1924. This arrest is a political offense, and she hopes that the Chinese government will provide protection for naturalized Korean residents. Jin went to the Japanese Consulate twice yesterday to visit Lee, but was not allowed to see him due to a ban on visits. However, the guard told Jin that Lee needed a change of underwear, which he needed, or that he was already suffering.

Inspection Teams for the Railway Exhibition Returned to Shanghai One After Another. The Opening of Through Train Service between Beiping and Shanghai Was Advanced to the 20th. The National Transportation Responsibility Will Begin on the 2nd of Next Month 145

According to the Central News Agency, the second National Railway Products Exhibition held by the Ministry of Railways in Nanjing, to which the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations invited various organizations and groups from the city to visit, departed at 8:00 AM on the 12th with over 40 people. They arrived at 2:00 PM and took cars prepared by the capital to the exhibition site at the Chinese YMCA on Zhonghua Road to visit. The scale of this exhibition is even greater than the first. The details are as follows:

Welcome from the Ministry of Railways 146

Yu Yanxian, Director of the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways, led the visit. A welcome tea party was held in the auditorium of the YMCA. Director Yu and Deputy Director of the Business Department Tan Yaozong delivered speeches, stating that the Ministry of Railways is holding this exhibition to raise awareness among merchants and the public, promote domestic goods sales, develop the national economy, increase railway transportation, and balance supply and demand. They also explained that they will make every effort to make railway operations more commercialized, implement responsible transportation of freight cars, and various joint transportation plans. This joint transportation method will actively seek cooperation with merchants and the public, expanding from a partial to a national scale. The through train service plan between Shanghai and Beiping, connecting national transportation and crossing the Yangtze River, was originally scheduled for the 22nd, but has now been changed to the 20th. The opening ceremony will be held on the 29th. This is the only major project in the Far East railway business, and all sectors of the country should pay close attention to it.

Visiting the Pavilions 147

When the reporter visited, starting from the Beining Pavilion, they then visited the first pavilion of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, the Tianjin-Pukou Pavilion, the Daokou-Qinghua Pavilion, the second pavilion of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, the Pinghan Pavilion, the Central Pavilion, the Jiaoji Pavilion, and the Longhai Pavilion. The products were excellent and the variety was abundant. One could only feel overwhelmed by the beauty. With such exquisite and numerous products in our country, and the current economic situation in such an irretrievable state, we must first rely on the efforts of the railway transportation industry in order to achieve increasing prosperity. The minerals and agricultural products of the Pinghan Line, and the various items in the crafts section, the coal, cotton, tobacco leaves, silk cocoons, ramie yarn, and woven goods of the Jiaoji Line, the fine art items of Weixian, the porcelain and ceramic ware of Boshan, and flour, cotton yarn, and kerosene, etc., are particularly prosperous, enough to make people happy and amazed. The excellent agricultural and industrial products of other provinces along the railway lines are also displayed in thousands, making it impossible to see them all. With such abundant resources and suffering from poverty, it further proves that the Chinese people are not working hard enough and are failing to live up to these natural resources.

Visiting the Ferry 148

Next, Director Yu introduced the great project of the Yangtze River ferry for through train service between Shanghai and Beiping. The magnificent buildings on both sides of the Yangtze River ferry stand majestically on the Jiangbin between Xiaguan and Pukou. The construction of the docks is equipped with an elevated bridge similar to the Yellow River Bridge at the top. Each dock itself is divided into sections. When the Yangtze River tide rises or falls, each dock section has an elevator that can be rotated at any time to keep the height of the dock from the water surface consistent. As for the railway tracks, they are particularly rare insurance tracks nationwide, with two lines lined up and the wheels running in the middle, making it difficult to derail. The structure is particularly strong and unparalleled. There is also a "protective dock" to prevent the movement of the ferry when it is docked. As for the ferry project, it has now been completed, costing 4 million yuan afterwards. The Changjiang ferry alone cost £180,000. It is reported that after the Pingpu Road opens to traffic on the 20th of this month and officially opens on the 29th, all passenger transport from Beiping to Shanghai will only take 26 hours for one round trip, eliminating the inconvenience of boat travel. It is truly the most convenient thing for travellers.

Responsible Joint Transportation 149

According to Director Yu, the Ministry of Railways has decided to implement responsible joint transportation starting from the 1st of next month. Once this responsible joint transportation is implemented, for any freight entrusted to the Railway Bureau for delivery, all procedures en route will be the responsibility of the Ministry of Railways. The cargo owner does not need to bother at all, which is particularly convenient for commercial transportation. Deputy Director Tan's pamphlet "A Small Handbook of Procedures for Railway Freight Transportation: What Farmers, Industry, Businessmen, and All Sectors Must Know" explains it in detail. There are also the "General Rules for Responsible Transportation of Freight Cars," "Documents and Forms for Responsible Transportation of Freight Cars," "Regulations for Bills of Lading for Responsible Transportation of Freight Cars," "Detailed Rules for Handling Bills of Lading," and "Styles of Bills of Lading," "Table of Classification of Ordinary Goods," and other books for reference.

Returning to Shanghai One After Another 150

The visiting group returned to Shanghai in two batches. The first batch returned on the night train on the 13th as scheduled by the Railway Bureau. The second batch, with the consent of Director Yu after discussion among most of the group members, changed to a special train at 8:00 AM on the 14th to return. The reporter returned to Shanghai on the 14th, accompanied by only 20 or so people, who were still hosted by the Ministry of Railways. Each person was given a flower to wear on their lapel as a sign. The Ministry of Railways also gave each person more than a dozen kinds of publications. Their hospitality was truly touching. However, when the train passed through Suzhou, unfortunately, two people were crushed to death on the tracks, causing the train to arrive in Shanghai as late as 3:30 PM.

After the Sharp Drop in the Silk Market, Two-Thirds of Silk Factories Have Suspended Operations. Employers Demand a Reduction in Workers' Wages. The Social Affairs Bureau Has Scheduled Mediation for Tomorrow 152

After the sharp drop in the European and American silk markets, the price of Jiangzhe factory silk B-grade has fallen from 920 yuan per dan to 700 yuan. The silk factories in the city that are still operating are suffering huge losses on the silk they produce. They have suspended operations one after another. The silk factories that are struggling to maintain operations, after discussion by the industry association, in addition to canceling the application for the Monday worship reward and the moth-related rewards, are also petitioning the competent authorities to reduce the wages of female workers from five jiao per day to four jiao and two fen in order to maintain the current situation. After receiving the report, the Social Affairs Bureau immediately sent staff to carefully investigate the silk prices in order to serve as a reference during mediation. It has also scheduled to convene the silk factory industry association and silk reeling industry for questioning at 2:00 PM on the 16th of this month to conduct mediation in accordance with the law. According to a survey conducted by a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency at the silk factory industry association, it is known that in July of this year, after the silk market picked up, the number of silk factories operating in the city, including the South City, Zhabei, and Hongkou Concession, totaled 64. After the sharp drop in the silk market, as of yesterday, only 20 silk factories in the city were still operating with difficulty.

The National Products Movement Exhibition jointly organized by the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' United Association and the Chinese National Products Merchants United Association opened on the 15th of last month. The temporary market will also close at 9:00 PM tonight. There will be entertainment day and night to enhance the guests' enjoyment.

Yesterday, the Electric Company Workers Issued a Public Letter: Reactions to the Company's Open Letter 157

The striking workers of the Shanghai Electric Company, in response to the Shanghai Electric Company's open letter, yesterday issued a public letter stating: "To all public organizations, banks, factories, companies, merchants, and Chinese and foreign residents who use electricity in Shanghai,

Greetings. The Shanghai Electric Company, in order to avoid the blame from all sectors for improper arrangements leading to a labor strike, has used the means of public apology and issued an open letter to seek support. However, the facts are undeniable and cannot be cunningly defended. Therefore, we hereby clarify the following:

(1) The first item in the open letter states that the increase in price is 3.6%, while the increase in wages for Chinese staff has reached 20.6%. However, according to the facts, any user knows that calculated according to the method during the era of the Public Works Department, the increase is 9.09%. Furthermore, if the wage increase for Chinese staff is calculated at 20.6%, then for workers whose wages were 50 yuan during the Public Works Department era, it should now be 63 yuan. However, the daily wages of ordinary workers, who previously earned 50 yuan, are now only 51 yuan, an increase of only 2% when calculated as a percentage. From this fact, it can be seen that the company is deceiving the public and attempting to evade responsibility.

(2) The second item in the open letter states that since 1928, the company has laid off 21.6% of its foreign staff and 18.1% of its Chinese staff. This is the company openly admitting to dismissing Chinese and foreign staff. It is also the company admitting to violating the agreement on the handover from the Public Works Department, which guaranteed that Chinese staff would enjoy the same stable service rights as they did during the Public Works Department era, and violating the announcement by the General Engineer and Manager Mr. O'lchie, which guaranteed that Chinese staff would enjoy the same service and rights as they did during the Public Works Department era. (The announcement is recorded below.) As for the dismissal of foreign staff, it is unknown whether it was due to the expiration of contracts. If it was not due to the expiration of contracts and foreign staff were dismissed, then like the dismissed Chinese staff, the company refuses to pay the due pension on the pretext of this. Therefore, we also stand on the position of those who have served the company for a long time, regardless of Chinese or foreign nationality, and have made contributions, to speak out against injustice. The Shanghai General Labor Union's report points out the different treatment of Chinese and foreign staff, and it is clear that the company's methods for ensuring the electricity business have not been improved, and there is a deliberate intention to reduce the value of the service of Chinese staff and not give them the same proportional treatment. It is not that the rights of foreign staff are being suppressed. The reason for the unfairness is not that foreign staff are gaining more benefits, but that Chinese staff are being deprived of the benefits they deserve, and the company is not understanding the modern management methods for protecting public utilities, which makes the electricity business, on which the public interest depends, unable to develop safely. Therefore, what it says in the second item is not enough to clarify that its dismissal of more than 400 Chinese staff and its refusal to pay the 5% reward on the pretext are reasonable. This is irrelevant, and the facts are very clear.

(3) The third item in the open letter states that the company not only pays all the rewards entrusted by the Public Works Department, but also that the current rewards set by the company are more generous than before. The Shanghai General Labor Union has admitted in its published report that the current reward system set by the company is indeed better than before. As for the statement that all rewards have been paid, it is purely deceptive. Fan Lisheng, Pan Genlin, Ni Wenfeng, Chen Baogen, Zhang Caisheng, who were previously dismissed by the company for representing workers in negotiations with the company, and Qiu Binggen, Dai Renheng, and Xue Abao, who were recently dismissed without reason, have not received any rewards from the company to this day, except for wages. Among the more than 400 workers who were previously dismissed, there are even more who have not yet received the rewards they deserve. May we ask if the company can list the names of all the dismissed workers and provide evidence of receiving the rewards?

(4) The fourth and fifth items in the open letter are not disputes in the company's manufacturing of the labor strike issue and need not be argued.

(5) The seventh item in the open letter states that the workers went on strike without reason or warning, and that it did not receive any requests beforehand. This statement is false and does not need to be refuted by our colleagues. The Shanghai General Labor Union's report has already explained it in detail. Here, we extract the facts as the following proof: (A) The first time, Fan Lisheng, Zhu Haoshen, Jiang Zhengming, and Ni Zhifu, representing the workers, negotiated with the company and were received by Vice President Mr. Scheld, but there was no sincere expression of discussion of the request. The second time they went to negotiate, they were rejected and Fan Lisheng was dismissed as a result. After that, all the foremen went to request it, but were also rejected. On July 3 of this year, for the pension issue, Ni Wenfeng, Pan Genlin, Zhang Caisheng, and Chen Baogen were again sent as representatives to negotiate, but not only were they rejected, but the four representatives were dismissed. In the middle of the question, the colleagues again signed their names to request acceptance, but were also rejected. (B) At the request of the labor union, party and government agencies sent representatives to investigate the company twice and indicated their willingness to mediate, but the company did not accept. (C) Zhu Xuefan and Shao Xubai, members of the Shanghai General Labor Union, in order to implement the Shanghai General Labor Union's recently adopted plan to encourage workers to work with peace of mind and dissuade strikes, separately invited Mr. Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and Chinese directors Yuan and Xu Xinliu, to seek opinions from the company out of personal friendship to mediate, but were rejected by the company authorities due to their preconceived ideas and firm attitude. (D) Mr. Zhongjie, the president of the Public Works Department, at the request of more than 200 workers' representatives to mediate and driven by a sense of responsibility for managing municipal affairs, also discussed with the company ways to eliminate disputes and mediate properly, but was also rejected by the company authorities due to their preconceived ideas and firm attitude. The above are all facts that the colleagues tried their best to avoid using the strike warning before implementing the strike warning. As for the transformation from a strike warning to a strike, it was caused by the company's deliberate intensification of the facts by closing the factory gates and refusing entry after the strike warning.

(6) The sixth, eighth, ninth, tenth, and eleventh items in the open letter and the explanations attached to the second item are all intended to impose unwarranted crimes on the colleagues and the leaders who guide the colleagues in good faith by fabricating facts or making worthless speculation, and to publicly provoke those who have prepared enough workers to maintain power generation services, those who advise power generation workers not to participate in the strike from the Shanghai General Labor Union, and those who order firefighters to resume work for the sake of public safety and to prevent fire alarms.

In short, this labor strike was actually provoked by the company's refusal to accept the prior requests of the colleagues due to its preconceived ideas and its refusal to accept the good intentions of all parties to mediate. As for the future actions of the colleagues, they should still, within the scope of their ability, take care of the interests of Chinese and foreign electricity users throughout the city and the safety and tranquility of society, respectfully abide by the advice of the Shanghai General Labor Union, and that power generation workers and firefighters who have resumed work should not participate in the strike, endure humiliation and pain, and not cause any changes, in order to await social justice. It is hoped that social organizations and Chinese and foreign users will assist the colleagues with reasonable opinions, implement the advice of the Shanghai General Labor Union to guide the striking workers to obey the order and suppress their anger, and that the completion of the work will not sit idly by and allow the forces of life requirements to rise up and instigate anger, causing the Shanghai General Labor Union and its colleagues to lose their authority to persuade, and to avoid the occurrence of incidents that are useless to society. This is a blessing for society, and also a blessing for the colleagues and striking workers who are now serving in accordance with the order with pain. We express our opinions with tears and plead with humility. We hope that everyone will take a public view.

Before the above opinions were released, they were actually shown to all the workers and signed by each worker with their consent. The original of this signature is being photographed and sent to the Shanghai General Labor Union to prove the verification of the previous facts to all sectors. Publicly announced by more than 2,000 workers of the Shanghai Electric Company who were forced to strike.

Attached is the announcement of the former General Engineer and General Manager O'lchie: To all staff, since the proposal of the Public Works Department was rejected at the taxpayers' meeting, I now know that the staff are afraid that all their interests will be harmed, and that their future service in Shanghai will not be as stable as under the Public Works Department. Therefore, they are panicked. I think you may not have understood the guarantee method stipulated in Article 14 of the special charter planned and announced by the Special Electricity Board (organized in 1929). I hereby solemnly declare that in the discussions between the Special Electricity Board and the three groups that purchased the Electricity Department, extra attention was paid to your interests and to protecting the future status of each staff member, just as it was under the Public Works Department, without any changes. The representatives of the American and Foreign Power Company also assured me that they had no intention of replacing staff. I know that there is a suspicion among the staff, that is, whenever a company takes over the Electricity Department, it must send its own personnel to replace positions such as those of Qi Qi. However, the company guarantees that this will never happen. You should know that I have no intention of trying to transfer the staff who have helped me to build this effective agency. The American and Foreign Power Company is well aware of the unexpected panic of the current staff, so it sent a telegram to reduce it. This telegram has been handed over to me by the company's representative in Shanghai. I hereby copy a copy and attach it later. Signed by the General Engineer and General Manager O'lchie, April 24, 1929.

Letter from Mr. Mou Fei, representative of the American and Foreign Power Company in Shanghai, to Mr. O'lchie: I have received the following telegram from Mr. Mi Queer, Minister of the Electricity Company's Supervision Department and Minister of the American and Foreign Power Company's Supervision Department, and Mr. Erte, General Manager of the American and Foreign Power Company: "Mr. Mou Fei, please forward this telegram to Mr. O'lchie. Our international group pays its respects to Mr. O'lchie and the well-being of his staff and welcomes them as members of our group. Regarding the future of each staff member in Shanghai, we will fully protect it and believe that under the new company's name, they should still work together to enable the public to continue to benefit." Because I cannot personally see each staff member, please convey my sincerity, welcome, and protection to everyone. Signed by Mou Fei, representative of the American and Foreign Power Company in Shanghai, April 22, 1929.

Labor Union Petition 159

The Northwest Intermodal Transport Officially Opens on November 1 164

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's intermodal transport on the Longhai Railway is of great importance to the shipping industry. Due to insufficient arrangements, it has been changed to be implemented next month. The details are recorded as follows.

Survey Situation 165

The bureau sent Wu Delin and Zhang Huanwen to Xilian Island to survey and determine the new wharf and arrange the lighters. Yesterday, Zhang sent a telegram to Shanghai, briefly stating that the old kiln's berthing and customs declaration matters had been negotiated with the Jiaohai Customs, and the customs had temporarily sent an officer to reside in the area for the bureau's ships to handle customs clearance. Permission has been granted to facilitate the matter. As for the establishment of a ship wharf in the kiln, due to the recent bad weather and excessive wind and waves, only six piles have been driven. Construction will resume after the weather improves, and it is expected to be completed next month. The accommodation materials for the warehouse workers have been transported and can be built quickly. The water depth at both ends of Xilian Island and Donglian Island is estimated to be 14 feet deep. If there is a northwest wind, the ship can berth at Donglian Island, and if there is a northeast wind, it can stop at Xilian Island, which is more stable.

The Track is About to be Completed 166

Most of the branch line of the old kiln railway laid on the Longhai Railway has been completed, and only one kilometer remains to be completed. The railway bureau is rushing to build it day and night to complete it all within October. After that, the loading and unloading of goods can directly reach the river bank, without the need for transshipment and carrying.

Warehouse Issues 167

However, there is one extremely difficult problem, which is the warehouse workers in that place. The bureau has decided to send workers from Shanghai, but the local workers in the old kiln have heard the news and expressed their opposition, resolutely refusing to allow the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to send other workers to the area. Zhang Wu and others sent a telegram to Shanghai for instructions. Yesterday afternoon, the bureau also replied, ordering them to consult with the Longhai Railway Bureau to achieve the purpose of sending their own workers. Zhang's telegram stated that he had personally gone to Zhengzhou to discuss the matter with the local authorities of the railway.

Sailing Next Month 168

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has approved the Longhai intermodal transport to officially send ships to operate from November 1. It is temporarily designated that the same ship and one chartered ship will operate. The wharf and warehouse, etc., will be completed by the end of the month. Yesterday, the H Bureau also telegraphed Zhang and others, urging them to proceed in the old kiln and not delay any further, because the ship schedule has already been arranged.

Industry Competition 169

Private Chinese shipping companies are determined to compete with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for navigation on the intermodal transport. If there is a shortage of ships, each bureau will send shifts, and the Sanbei Company will open a Guangdong route at this time to take the lead. Yu Qiaqing will host a banquet for various Hakka people from Guangdong in the next day or two to solicit freight.

The Coast Patrol Office Moves Back to Wusong 170

The National Coast Patrol Office of Wusong Fort Taiwan is an important agency of the Navy. The position of director is filled by Wu Zhennan. Whenever piracy or other disasters occur along the coast, the office can dispatch fleets to suppress them. After the January 28 Incident in Shanghai, all the buildings of the office were destroyed. It temporarily moved to the Hydrographic Survey Bureau in the Xinxiqu area of Longhua, Shanghai, to work. It has now been rebuilt with funds allocated by the Ministry of the Navy and has been completed. Therefore, the office has now moved back to its original site in Wusong and started working.

Japanese Merchants Resume North China Shipping: One of the Reasons for the Relaxation of Resistance and the Infiltration of Inferior Goods 171

After the January 28 Incident, Japanese ships on the North China line suspended their schedules and stopped sailing due to the impact of resistance. Since January and February of this year, there has been a daily increase in the number of inferior goods shipped to North China. The Dalian Steamship Company specially decided to resume the regular passenger ship route on the Shanghai-Tianjin line to compete with our country's shipping companies in the North China shipping industry. It has been decided to specially dispatch the 1,300-ton passenger ship Tianhumaru to operate from the 16th of this month. Another ship will be added later.

The Quanzhang Guild Donates 10,000 Yuan for Aviation; Other Donations are Also Huge 172

The Shanghai Solicitation Team Headquarters of the Chinese Aviation Association is rushing to complete its closure, but people from all walks of life are enthusiastically donating huge amounts of money for the aviation salvation movement. In the past few days, the office has received a donation of 10,000 yuan from the Quanzhang Guild. Team Leader Lu Zhengbing of the 250th Team has raised 1,131 yuan and 29 cents. Mr. Zhou Zhonglin, a member of the New Zealand Wellington Aviation Association, donated 5 pounds in British currency.

Municipal Government Rejects Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Request for Exemption of Jiangwan Boat Tax 180

The Shanghai Municipal Government, regarding the Jiangwan boat tax case, replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Your submission has been received. The Jiangwan waterway connects Wusong in the east and Dachang in the west, serving as a vital route for ships entering the city. The boat tax is therefore very important and cannot be easily waived. These boats, as they operate within the city's rivers, intercepting goods and sailing, should be registered and taxed according to regulations without any doubt. As for the Wusong small carts, a temporary exemption of six months was granted because these carts are owned by local villagers and used for personal transportation, limited to the Wusong area. This is different in nature from boats transporting goods and occupying the city's rivers. Furthermore, from October onwards, the small carts must still be taxed according to regulations. The request to exempt Jiangwan boat tax based on the precedent of not taxing local villagers raising cattle, sheep, and pigs for plowing and transportation, but taxing them upon slaughter, is difficult to approve. This reply is hereby issued for your information."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Convenes Industrial Research Conference 181

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of the Industrial Research Committee at 3:00 PM on the 11th. Attendees included Zheng Chengqing, Yang Qingsheng, Hu Xiyuan, Chen Xiaodie, Zhou Xiangsheng, Xiang Shengwu, Lu Wenshao, Gu Xinyi, and Shen Huachen. Mr. Hu Xiyuan was elected as the chairman. The following items were discussed: (1) An investigation into the types of industrial products and sources of industrial raw materials used by various factories in the city. It was resolved to send personnel to investigate all factories in Shanghai and compile the findings into a publication for reference by various organizations and groups. (2) Organizing an industrial inspection tour to conduct on-site observations both domestically and internationally for the purpose of learning and improvement. It was resolved to approve this in principle, and to formulate detailed plans for implementation when needed. (3) Implementing scientific management methods in all factories in the city and having the Chamber of Commerce send personnel to guide and assist in this process. It was resolved to approve this and to cooperate with the Technical Cooperation Association in its implementation. (4) All products from domestic goods factories should clearly indicate the manufacturer in Chinese characters, and foreign characters should not be used exclusively to avoid confusion and ensure recognition. It was resolved that, in addition to those already using both Chinese and English, those using only English should be requested to add Chinese. (5) Protecting the production volume and registered trademarks of domestic goods factories. It was resolved that each committee member would draft their opinions, which would then be compiled and discussed to create specific measures. (6) Holding regular meetings every fourth Wednesday afternoon of each month at 2:00 PM. It was resolved to approve and implement this.

News Censorship Bureau Inspects Social News; Central Propaganda Committee Sends Letter to Municipal Party Headquarters for Compliance 183

According to the National Press, Mr. Feng Yixian, the executive director of the Education Association of the Six Districts of this city, previously submitted a report to the Municipal Education Bureau regarding the unrestrained descriptions of obscene events between men and women in social news published in various newspapers in the city, which he believed were detrimental to social morals. He requested that measures be taken to ban them. The bureau, after receiving the letter, considered the matter to be of great importance to the future of the nation and the people, and since this city is a focal point for both Chinese and foreigners, it was detrimental to the national image. Therefore, it specially invited representatives from the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus to discuss solutions, and decided to send a letter to the Municipal Party Headquarters to forward to the central government, requesting the revision of news censorship standards to include social news in order to thoroughly eliminate this problem. The original report has already been published in previous newspapers. It is now reported that the Central Propaganda Committee, in addition to adding a clause regarding "the retention or deletion of social morality news" to the news censorship standards, which was submitted to the Central Standing Committee for approval on the 5th of this month, also sent a special letter to the Municipal Party Headquarters of this city for compliance. The original letter is copied below: "To the direct addressee, the Central Executive Committee Secretariat forwarded a document from your committee to the central government, requesting the amendment of news censorship standards and the banning of obscene records to maintain morality. The Propaganda Committee, etc., reviewed and considered that banning obscene records in newspapers is indeed essential. The original proposer, Feng Yixian, cares about social morality and his suggestions are insightful. However, the news censorship standards have already been revised, adding a clause regarding 'the retention or deletion of social morality news,' which was submitted to the Central Standing Committee for approval on the 5th of this month. This letter is specially sent for your information, and to commend the original proposer. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee." It is reported that after receiving the letter, the department proposed it at the 93rd regular meeting and resolved to commend the original proposer and send a letter to the Education, Public Security, and Social Affairs Bureaus for compliance.

Four Kidnappers From Tianjin to Shanghai Sentenced to Death; Geng Huatang Committed Suicide and the Judgment Was Not Accepted; Li Yueshan and Three Other Bandits Sent to the First Special Court 184

Jin Jiulin, Inspector of the Special Agency of the French Concession Police Department, along with Head Detectives Zhang Ziying and Qian Yumin, Deputy Detectives Zhou Bingcheng and Zhou Yaoting, and Detectives Cui Zhenguo, Qin Youyu, and Cai Jinzhang, etc., arrested prominent kidnapping kingpins Zheng Tangsheng (also known as Guan Shengsheng), Shang Zhen, Liu Yimin, Wu Shaoting, Geng Huatang, Li Yueshan, Fang Qingshan, and suspects Yu Yuanzhou, Chang Jianxi, Wang Shikong, Bian Zengyan, and a woman named Zheng Chenshi, totaling twelve men and women, in Tianjin in July of this year. They were transferred to Shanghai. Also, Cao Ziqing and Li Youren, two related individuals, were brought from the First Special District Prison in the Public Concession. It was found that from 1928 to February of this year, the bandits successively kidnapped Huang Yuyi, the deputy director of the Zhongnan Bank, Chen Yanghe, the deputy manager of the Siming Bank, Ze Lin, the son of Yunnan Division Commander Gu Zizhen, He Shaoting, the owner of the Xinsenji Construction Factory, Huang Baohua, a major dye merchant, etc., in this city, extorting huge sums of money for their release. They also kidnapped Chen Zhuling and Liang Huiwu, two compradores of Jardine Matheson in Tianjin, tore up the tickets, buried the bodies, and eliminated the evidence. They also strangled their accomplice, Xiao Shaoxing. Furthermore, when kidnapping Huang Yuyi, they shot and killed Huang's chauffeur and injured two guards. They also suspected that Wu Kunshan, a representative sent by Huang's family to negotiate the ransom, embezzled the ransom money and lured Wu to Zhongshan Road and shot him to death. These serious cases were transferred to the Second Special District Local Court, and public prosecutions were filed based on the Regulations for the Suppression of Bandits and the crime of murder. After a trial presided over by Li Changnian, the suspects Yu Yuanzhou, Chang Jianxi, Wang Shikong, Bian Zengyan, and Zheng Chenshi, whom the police department did not prosecute, were released first. The nine defendants, Zheng, Shang, Liu, Wu, Geng, Li, Fang, Cao, and Li, were remanded in custody to await further trial. However, Geng Huatang, fearing punishment, hanged himself in the police station detention center on the 1st of this month. Later, the two inmates, Zheng and Shang, learned of Geng's suicide and also attempted suicide at the same time. Fortunately, the guards discovered them early and rescued them, sending them to the hospital for treatment. On the 9th of this month, a continued hearing was held, and the debate was declared closed, with a date set for sentencing. All these details have been published in previous newspapers. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. At 9:00 AM, the police department escorted the defendants to the court. Judge Li presided over the criminal court and ordered the defendants to be brought to the court. After a brief interrogation, the main text of the judgment was announced: Zheng Tangsheng was sentenced to death for continuous kidnapping and extortion, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. He was also sentenced to two years of imprisonment for receiving stolen goods, to be executed concurrently with the death penalty, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. Shang Zhen was sentenced to death for continuous kidnapping and extortion, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. Liu Yimin was sentenced to death for continuous kidnapping and extortion, with permanent deprivation of civil rights, and to life imprisonment for joint murder, to be executed concurrently with the death penalty, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. Wu Shaoting was sentenced to death for continuous kidnapping and extortion, with permanent deprivation of civil rights, and to life imprisonment for assisting in murder, to be executed concurrently with the death penalty, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. Li Yueshan was sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment for continuous kidnapping and extortion, with deprivation of civil rights for fifteen years. Cao Ziqing, Li Youren, and Fang Qingshan were found not guilty. The prosecution of Geng Huatang was not accepted. A check for 1,300 yuan from the Qunye Bank (found on Zheng Tangsheng) was confiscated. The defendants were all returned to the detention center to await further instructions. After the judgment, bailiffs from the First Special District Court presented an official document requesting that the defendants be transferred for interrogation. The judge ruled that since the four defendants, Zheng, Shang, Liu, and Wu, had already been sentenced to death, there was no need for transfer, but Li Yueshan, Cao Ziqing, and Li Youren were allowed to be transferred for interrogation.

Continued Trial of the Huge Customs Clerk Fraud Case; Complete Interrogation of Witnesses Yesterday; Emphasis on the Organization of the Customs 185

Customs clerks and unscrupulous merchants organized the Hezhong Company, fraudulently evading millions in customs duties. Nine defendants, including Su Kunnian, Shi Cunqiao, Wang Yueren, Wei Anxiang, Jiang Genhan, Zhang Qiutao, Sun Guozhang, Chen Zhongshan, and Chen Guoliang, were detained by the local court and prosecuted. At 2:00 PM yesterday, Judge Qian Chengjun continued the trial. The defendants were represented by lawyers Qu Yue, Yao Jiapeng, Zhang Enhua, and E Sen. The Jianghai Customs was represented by lawyer Jiang Yiping, who also filed a private prosecution. Those summoned included Deputy Tax Commissioner Schubert, Assistant Zhuang Zezong, Peng Shi, the head of the Water Patrol Police Criminal Division, and Chinese Detective Cheng Yongnian, etc. The official questioned Zhuang Zezong, 37 years old, from Shanghai, currently serving as an assistant in the anti-smuggling section of the Customs. He was asked if he was familiar with the general affairs department of the Customs. He replied that he had worked there before. He was asked if most imports and exports are declared for tax. He replied yes. He was asked if the case involved import taxes. He replied yes. He was asked where the import tax declaration process starts. He replied, the Valuation Section, and then it is sent to the General Affairs Department for tax assessment. He was asked where the assessment is done. He replied, the Tax Assessment Counter, but it must first go through the Warehouse Receipt Counter. He was asked what they do. He replied, the Warehouse Receipt Counter removes the numbers, while the Tax Assessment Counter collects taxes based on the documents, issues tax payment certificates, and then sends them to the Waiting Room for issuance, which completes the tax payment. The tax is paid at the Central Bank's office. He was asked where it goes after the tax payment certificate is issued. He replied, the Tax Collection and Storage Counter. He was asked where it goes after that. He replied, it is then filed by the clerks. He was asked about the supervision counter. He replied, that is the head of the import department. He was asked how far away it is. He replied, very close. He was asked how many cases there are in total. He replied, fifty-eight cases, mostly involving fraud by the Hezhong Company. At this point, lawyer Jiang Yiping stated that initially, genuine declaration forms were replaced with fake ones when the tax was not paid, so some genuine forms were actually fake, and some fake forms had genuine stamps. Therefore, some of the existing archived files and some of the documents found in the Hezhong Company had fake stamps, so it was entirely copied from the Hezhong Company. The official questioned Xu Zihan, a customs tax official for 13 years. He was asked if he was related to Zhang Qiutao. He replied no. He was asked where he works. He replied, the Import Tax Payment Counter. He was asked where Zhang Qiutao works. He replied, he works at my counter, but he is a clerk. He was asked if Zhang Qiutao ever argued with someone in black clothing. He replied he did not notice. At this point, Wan Shougen testified that he was a clerk in the Customs Document Sorting Room. He was asked what Sun Guozhang does. He replied, I order the declaration forms and he takes them away. He was asked if there is a fixed number of declaration forms ordered. He replied, there is no fixed number, hundreds for thick stacks, a few for thin stacks, there is no fixed standard. I only order, and I don't know the number. He was asked if the tax is paid when ordering the declaration forms. He replied it is already paid. He was asked if fake forms are inserted when ordering the declaration forms. He replied, I don't know. He was asked how the declaration forms are stolen. He replied, I am on the third floor, I don't know, etc. At this point, the official announced that the case would be adjourned for two weeks for further interrogation. The defendants were all returned to custody. All the evidence, after being numbered and explained by lawyer Jiang Yiping, was submitted for review.

The Truth About Ji A'gen's Gun and Axe Attack; Wei A'gen's Improper Behavior; Old Man Sends People to Murder Him 186

Ji A'gen, a coppersmith from Jiangbei, 27 years old, lived at 57 Yuqing Lane, Gonghe Road, Zhabei. Unexpectedly, around 5:00 AM the day before yesterday, while A'gen and his wife, Wang, were sound asleep, five assailants suddenly arrived, each wielding a handgun and a sharp axe, and simultaneously attacked Ji with guns and axes. He was struck by four axes and one bullet to the nose. The assailants fled the scene immediately. The Second Branch of the Fourth District Police Station sent Ji to the hospital, where his condition was critical. Details have already been published in this newspaper. After the incident, various rumors circulated in the vicinity. Some said that Ji's friends, Ma and Guo, were both in love with the same woman, and were competing for her affections. Ji mediated between them, and as a result, the woman went to Ma. However, Guo still maintained a secret relationship with the woman, which was discovered by Ji, who questioned Guo, causing Guo to become angry and commit this vicious act. However, only last night did someone discover the truth. It turns out that Ji's "Old Man," a certain Jia, is a well-known figure among the gangsters in Zhabei, with a penchant for women, having as many as four concubines. Ji was originally a beloved disciple of Jia. Unexpectedly, someone recently sowed discord in front of Jia, claiming that Ji was having an affair with Jia's third concubine, creating a scandalous relationship disguised as a teacher-disciple bond. This angered Jia greatly, but on the surface, he could not openly break ties. Therefore, he secretly sent many of his followers to carry out this vicious attack on Ji. Currently, the Second Branch of the Fourth District Police Station is thoroughly investigating the case.

Large Group of Workers on Qu Zhenren Road Clash Over Urination; Many Injured; Ten Assailants Arrested 187

Many textile factories are located in the Jinxiu Lane area of Zhizaoju Road in the Nanshi district, all employing workers from Anhui province. Yesterday morning at 9:30 AM, Zhou Daoguo, from Hefei, Anhui, was urinating next to the entrance of the Huiming Flashlight Battery Factory on Qu Zhenren Road when he was stopped by the factory's accountant, leading to a conflict. The security guard Yan Yinhe's attempt to mediate was unsuccessful. A large group of workers from Anhui then used axes, iron bars, and other weapons to injure several people and rob a No. 4479 rifle from the security team. Police officers from the Second District arrested ten assailants and recovered the stolen rifle. The details are as follows:

Cause of the Incident 188

The Huiming Flashlight Battery Factory at 585 Qu Zhenren Road, Zhizaoju Road, Nanshi, is owned by Ding Xiongzhao, a member of the Municipal Security Team from Wuxi, and others. It is a large-scale operation employing over sixty male and female workers, with a very successful business. However, the factory is located in a remote area, and people often urinate at the entrance, making it unsightly. Yesterday morning at 9:30 AM, Ding Shousong, the factory's accountant from Wuxi, saw Zhou Daoguo, an Anhui worker residing in Jinxiu Lane, Zhizaoju Road, urinating again at the factory entrance. Ding Shousong went to stop him, but Zhou refused, leading to a dispute. At that time, the flashlight factory workers were starting their shift and came out to stop him. The Anhui textile factory workers nearby, thinking that their fellow villager was being humiliated, blew a whistle and gathered their fellow workers, each carrying iron bars, axes, wooden sticks, etc., and attacked the flashlight factory workers, resulting in a major clash. Outnumbered, the battery factory workers reported to the First Defense Team of the Fifth Brigade of the Runan Road Security Team and requested assistance. Yan Yinhe, the team's guard, rushed to the scene to mediate with the Anhui workers after receiving the report, but the mediation was unsuccessful. The guard was slashed with an axe in several places and had a No. 4479 rifle stolen.

Large Number of Injuries 189

Arrest of Assailants 190

At that time, the Huining Road Police Station of the Second District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the First Defense Team of the Fifth Brigade of the Security Team urgently reported the situation to District Chief Police Officer Li by telephone and requested immediate dispatch of police to stop the violence and investigate the assailants. Nanjing Municipal Chamber of Commerce Petitions the Legislative Yuan to Amend the Partnership Article of the Civil Code, and Replies to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce for Information 193

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce previously telegraphed various chambers of commerce, requesting joint advocacy for the amendment of Article 681 of the Debt Section of the Civil Code, in response to a petition from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce. The Nanjing Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied yesterday, stating: "Respectfully replying, your previous telegram stated that the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce's letter argued that Article 681 of the Civil Code, which stipulates that partners are jointly responsible for partnership debts, is difficult to implement and requested joint advocacy and amendment by the Legislative Yuan. This has been received. The matter is of great importance to the future of commerce and must be strongly advocated to eliminate obstacles. In addition to submitting a petition to the Legislative Yuan for amendment, a copy of the petition is enclosed for your information. Respectfully addressed to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China." The enclosed copy of the petition to the Legislative Yuan states: "Petitioning for a matter. We believe that national legislation must be in harmony with the common customs of society in order to be implemented effectively. Achieving fairness ensures equal benefits and harms, while failing to do so reverses the balance. Therefore, matters concerning the business operations of merchants require careful consideration and legal protection. However, upon examining the current Article 681 of the Debt Section of the Civil Code, which states that if partnership assets are insufficient to settle partnership debts, the partners shall be jointly and severally liable for the deficit, we are deeply concerned and feel compelled to express our views. While the interests of partners in a business are inherently linked, there must be appropriate limitations. If profits are distributed according to shares, but losses result in unlimited joint and several liability, the rights and obligations are clearly disparate, lacking equality. The legislative intent seems solely to protect creditors' rights, without considering the potential burdens on partners in the future, which is somewhat unbalanced. As representatives of the commercial community of Nanjing, we feel obligated to speak out. We respectfully petition your honorable Yuan to review and approve the appropriate amendment of Article 681 of the Debt Section of the Civil Code to ensure fairness and promote commercial development. We eagerly await your decision." - Cao Gexian, Wu Zhenxiu, Mu Huaxuan, Ran Xizhang, Du Zhe'an, Standing Committee Members of the Reorganization Committee of the Nanjing Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

International Problems Research Association Discusses the Issue of Raw Silk Sales to the United States 194

The International Problems Research Association held a meeting at 4 Hong Kong Road at 6:00 PM the day before yesterday to discuss the issue of promoting raw silk sales to the United States. Mr. Miao Zhongxiu, the director of the Raw Silk Department of the Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, was invited to speak. More than ten people attended, including Guo Bingwen, Chen Liting, Cai Wuji, Li Zhaohuan, Cao Yunxiang, Chen Zheqing, Xu Fengshi, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Baohua, and Mei Qiju. After Chairman Guo Bingwen introduced Mr. Miao to speak, various issues were discussed, such as (1) establishing a raw silk promotion agency in the United States, (2) how to ensure that Chinese raw silk is readily available in the New York market, and (3) how to compete with Japan in terms of raw silk prices and quality. It was advocated that the government and businesses should jointly invest in improving sericulture and start handling promotion matters.

The International Trade Bureau Plans to Restore the Decline of National Silk by Establishing a Permanent Organization to Promote Sales Abroad 196

The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in order to promote the sale of Chinese silk abroad, previously convened representatives from major silk weaving factories in this city to discuss improvement measures at the bureau. It was decided to improve the quality of thin silk, conduct direct transactions, and not easily rely on foreign merchants to avoid being manipulated by them. It is now learned that although the silk factories have agreed to improve, the foreign market has not yet paid attention. Therefore, in addition to sending letters to chambers of commerce in Europe and the United States, it is also necessary to contact major silk factories to jointly form a permanent promotion organization in order to restore the decline of China's silk industry. It is currently in the planning stage, and once everything is ready, it will be officially organized and established.

Recent Improvements to the Shangchuan Bus Service 197

The Shangchuan long-distance bus, which runs between Qingning Temple in Pudong and Chuansha, originally took one and a half hours for each trip. Recently, the company replaced the steam engine, increasing the speed, and plans to shorten the travel time to one hour per trip to facilitate transportation. A trial run began on the 16th of last month to test the results. The assessment for one month has been smooth, so it has been decided to continue with this method. The company is also actively renovating the facilities at each station. It is planned to issue round-trip tickets after the Qingning Temple and Chuansha stations are renovated. It is said that the ticket price will be slightly discounted, saving passengers time and money, and they hope it will be implemented soon. It is also learned that due to the shortening of daylight hours, the company will, as usual, reduce one bus from Chuansha Station at 7:00 AM and 5:00 PM, and one bus from Qingning Temple Station at 8:00 AM and 6:00 PM, starting from October 16th. However, on Mondays, Chuansha Station will add a bus at 7:00 AM, and Qingning Temple Station will add a bus at 8:00 AM.

Du Yifang, the Main Culprit in the Case of Japanese Yarn Impersonating National Yarn, Has Still Not Been Apprehended, and the Case Could Not Be Heard Yesterday 199

Du Yifang, the owner of Lichangchunjisha, a yarn shop in Ruilin Lane, Aiduya Road, secretly sold "Lima Brand" Japanese yarn produced by the Japanese-owned Dakang Yarn Factory, pretending it was "Ren Zhong Brand" national yarn produced by the Shenxin Yarn Factory, and sold it to Dingxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory. He also altered the Lima Brand tax bill to Ren Zhong Brand, thus deceiving them. Later, Dingxin planned to transport the goods to Ningbo and requested the tax bureau to verify the transport permit, which led to the discovery. Sun Xinzhu, the manager of Dingxin, negotiated with Du, but Du shirked responsibility in every way. Sun then hired lawyer Min Ganghou to file a criminal self-accusation against Du, accusing him of forging tax bills, defrauding taxes, damaging reputation, and harming credit, and requesting severe punishment according to the law, as well as compensation for all losses. The First Special District Court has repeatedly summoned him, but the defendant has never appeared in court. It was ordered that the plaintiff be directed to arrest and bring the defendant to justice, which has been reported in this newspaper. Now, the plaintiff, Sun Xinzhu, has tried to investigate Du Yifang's hiding place, which is in the area under the jurisdiction of the Hongkou police station. The day before yesterday evening, Sun led detectives from the police station to the address secretly, but Du was well-informed and escaped in advance, so they returned empty-handed and failed to capture him. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi continued the hearing, and lawyer Min explained the situation and presented a letter, saying that this letter was sent by the defendant to the plaintiff from the post office, but the whereabouts of the defendant are still unknown. Judge Wu ruled that the case could not be heard yet and ordered that the defendant's address be ascertained and reported to the court before setting another hearing date.

Playing with a Handgun Causes Disaster, Ren Zhiqin Is Shot and Seriously Injured 202

Ren Zhiqin, from Fenghua, Zhejiang, is 18 years old and works as an accountant in the button department of the Dahua Military Clothing Factory in Yuqingli, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei. Yesterday morning, at around 11:30, Ren had nothing much to do, so he slowly walked to the factory gate to look around and sat down with a member of the security team stationed at the factory, chatting and laughing. While they were talking, the security team member took out his handgun to wipe it. When Ren saw it, he eagerly wanted to take the gun to play with it. The team member, knowing that there were six bullets in it, removed them. Unexpectedly, one bullet remained inside, which the team member did not notice at the time. When he pulled the trigger, a bullet suddenly fired out, hitting Ren Zhiqin below his left breast. He immediately fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. The team member was shocked and horrified when he suddenly caused the disaster. Fortunately, the workers in the factory heard the noise and came out to see. They quickly sent Ren to Baolong Hospital for treatment. The bullet has not yet been removed, and his life is in danger.

The Nanjing Film Review Committee, under the command of the Ministry of Education, plans to open this film together with the sports field during the National Games for the viewing of military and political dignitaries and athletes. Unfortunately, because Shanghai was showing this film at the time, it was not successful. The performance of the protagonist, Warner Krauss, is profound, resolute, sharp, and vivid, and he is indeed worthy of being a veteran of the European silver screen.

Aviation Lottery Draw Newsreel Premieres. The first phase of the Aviation Highway Construction Lottery was drawn at Yiyuan on July 31. Tens of thousands of people attended the event. A newsreel was filmed by "China Sound and Color Film Company," and the details of the event were vividly displayed. The film has been scheduled to premiere at the Central Grand Theater today. It is heard that the film is currently managed by the Dayun Company at No. 330 Sichuan Road. In order to promote the national consciousness of assisting national transportation construction, any theaters that intend to borrow the film before November 15 can contact Dayun Company directly. The rental fee will be waived, and the company will cover it itself.

Special Edition for the National Games of China

### Five National Records Broken on the Fifth Day of the National Games: Shanghai's Hao Chunde Wins, Wang Jihuai Second; Two Relay Races Also Set National Records; Thrilling Shanghai-Fujian Women's Basketball Match This Morning 214

(Nanjing, 14th) Today is the fifth day of the National Games. In the pentathlon, three more national records were broken, making it five sports in total. Shanghai's Hao Chunde won the championship with 3010.295 points, breaking the record. In the 1600-meter relay final, the Shanghai team set a new record with a time of 3 minutes 31.8 seconds. In the 400-meter relay preliminaries, both Shanghai and Guangdong set new records. Shanghai has secured the all-around championship. The ball game competitions have reached the quarter-finals and semi-quarter-finals, and the situation is tense. This morning, the Shanghai and Fujian women's basketball teams will compete for the quarter-final spot, promising a thrilling match.

### Shanghai's Hao Chunde Sets National Record in Pentathlon: 3010.295 Points; Shanghai's Wang Jihuai Second, Also Sets National Record 215

(Nanjing, 14th) The results of the pentathlon are: 1st place, Shanghai's Hao Chunde with 3010.295 points, a new national record; 2nd place, Shanghai's Wang Jihuai with 3001.700 points, also a new national record; 3rd place, Guangdong's Huang Yingjian with 2775.47 points; 4th place, Beijing's Zhong Jiqing with 2494.875 points. The top five results for the first half of the decathlon are: 1st place, Shanghai's Chen Baoqiu with 3156.70 points; 2nd place, Beiping's Zhang Lingjia with 3106.882 points; 3rd place, Shanghai's Chen Ling with 2907.7758 points; 4th place, Hebei's Zhao Enhui with 2901.345 points; 5th place, Shandong's Liu Mengling with 2693.330 points.

Ended in the Dimness of Night 216

There were 45 participants in the pentathlon. The competition was extremely complicated due to too many groups. It started in the afternoon and only finished at 7 PM. The 1500-meter event in the afternoon was held in near darkness. A lamp was placed around the field, and the starter and finish line judges used lights as signals. It was truly a spectacle of an unprecedented competition. As a result of the competition, Shanghai's Hao Chunde won the championship, while Wang Jihuai finished second with a difference of eight points. Hao and Wang's scores both exceeded 3,000 points. Both Hao and Wang broke the national record. Hao and Wang are the first to break 3,000 points in the Chinese pentathlon. Hao's long jump in the first event did not reach his maximum potential. Hao's javelin throw in the first throw reached the highest record, and the 200-meter time of 23.2 seconds was also excellent. However, Hao's average in the discus and 1500-meter events was not as good as Wang Jihuai's. The scores of the third and fourth places were much lower than Hao and Wang's.

Still Lower than Far Eastern Record 217

The highest Far Eastern record is 2838 points, but this is based on the old scoring method, which is much lower than the current scoring method. Therefore, although Hao and Wang's scores exceed the Far Eastern record, they cannot be considered Far Eastern records. If Hao and Wang's scores were calculated using the old scoring method, they would still be far below the Far Eastern record.

### Shanghai Breaks National Record in 1600-Meter Relay Final: 3 Minutes 31.8 Seconds; Guangdong Team Also Breaks National Record in 400-Meter Relay Preliminary: 45.4 Seconds 218

(Nanjing, 14th) In the 1600-meter relay preliminary, which was changed to the final, Shanghai was second, 60 meters behind. Fujian was third, and Beijing was fourth. The time of 3 minutes 31.8 seconds is a new national record. In the 400-meter relay preliminary, which was divided into two groups, the first group was won by Guangdong, followed by Liaoning and Beijing, with a time of 45.4 seconds, a new national record. In the second group, Shanghai was first, followed by Beiping and Hebei. Shanghai's last runner, Hao Chunde, did not push hard for time, finishing in 45.6 seconds. In the final, they can beat Guangdong and create a better record.

### Shanghai Secure in All-Around Championship: Already Has 26 Points Yesterday 219

(Nanjing, 14th) With Hao and Wang already in the top two spots in the pentathlon, and the Shanghai team also winning the 1600-meter relay, the Shanghai team is secure in the all-around championship. As for the "Iron Bull" Chen Baoqiu, due to his good average scores in each event, he changed from the pentathlon to participate in the decathlon. His total score in the first half is the first, which is particularly commendable. The scores for the all-around competition yesterday are as follows:

Shanghai: 26 points

### Shanghai Sets New Record in 1600-Meter Relay Final: 3 Minutes 31.5 Seconds 221

(Nanjing, 14th) In the all-around competition, the 1600-meter relay race was originally scheduled to have three preliminary groups, but because only six teams participated, it was directly changed to the final. At the start, Beiping was in the lead, but the Shanghai team surpassed them in the second leg. The Beiping, Fujian, and Beijing teams were constantly changing positions, making the competition extremely fierce. By the third leg, the Shanghai team had surpassed them by 30 meters, and Zeng Rongzhong, the fourth leg runner, widened the lead to about 60 meters, advancing easily. As a result, Shanghai was first, Beiping was second, Fujian was third, and Beijing was fourth. The time of 3 minutes 31.5 seconds is a new national record. The Shanghai team members were Su Xiaoru in the first leg, Liu Fukang in the second leg, Li Yanxiang in the third leg, and Zeng Rongzhong in the fourth leg. The Beiping team members were Sun Yueming, Song Shuzhang, Peng Renbian, and Luo Qinglong. The Fujian team members were Dai Shuguo, Lin Shaozhou, Tian Yunyong, and Chen Xingzi. The Beijing team members were Ma Yu, Ge Chongkang, Hu Shixuan, and Yang Daogui.
